CockroachDB v23.2 <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/release-support-policy#support-types" data-versioned="true">(LTS)</a> is a required <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases#major-versions" data-versioned="true">Regular release</a>.

Refer to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/release-support-policy#support-types" data-versioned="true">Major release types</a> before installing or upgrading for release timing and support details. To learn what's new in this release, refer to its [Feature Highlights](#feature-highlights).

On this page, you can read about changes and find downloads for all production and testing releases of CockroachDB v23.2 <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/release-support-policy#support-phases" data-versioned="true">(LTS)</a>

- For key feature enhancements in v23.2 and other upgrade considerations, refer to the notes for [v23.2.0](#v23-2-0).
- For details about release types, naming, and licensing, refer to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases" data-versioned="true">Releases</a> page.
- Be sure to also review the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/release-support-policy" data-versioned="true">Release Support Policy</a>.
- After downloading a supported CockroachDB binary, learn how to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/install-cockroachdb" data-versioned="true">install CockroachDB</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upgrade-cockroach-version" data-versioned="true">upgrade your cluster</a>.

Get future release notes emailed to you:

<MarketoEmailForm />

## v23.2.29

Release Date: February 19, 2026

### Downloads

<Note>
Experimental downloads are not qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments, whether they are for testing releases or production releases.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.29
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.29 on Github, visit [v23.2.29 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.29).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.28...v23.2.29](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.28...v23.2.29)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a rare race condition between range splits and MVCC garbage collection where a GCRequest could target keys outside its declared span. In rare cases, this could result in data on the post-split right-hand side (RHS) being incorrectly garbage collected, potentially leading to lost writes. The system now detects and rejects such malformed GC requests. [#163775](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/163775)

### Performance improvements

- Lookup joins can now be used on tables with virtual columns even if the type of the search argument is not identical to the column type referenced in the virtual column. [#152926](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/152926)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.27
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.27 on Github, visit [v23.2.27 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.27).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.26...v23.2.27](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.26...v23.2.27)

### Operational changes

- The `goschedstats.always_use_short_sample_period.enabled` cluster setting should be set to `true` for any serious production cluster; this will prevent unnecessary queuing in admission control CPU queues. [#146742](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/146742)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug that could potentially cause a changefeed to complete erroneously when one of its watched tables encounters a schema change. [#147040](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/147040)
- Fixed a bug that caused the SQL Activity &gt; Statement Fingerprint page to fail to load details for statements run with application names containing a `#` character. [#147219](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/147219)
- Fixed a bug that could cause the `cockroach` process to `segfault` when collecting runtime execution traces (typically collected via the **Advanced Debug** page in the Console). [#147339](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/147339)
- Fixed a bug that could cause stable expressions to be folded in cached query plans. The bug could cause stable expressions like `current_setting` to return the wrong result if used in a prepared statement. The bug was introduced in v23.2.22, v24.1.14, v24.3.9, v25.1.2, and the v25.2 alpha. [#147456](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/147456)

### Performance improvements

- TTL jobs now respond to cluster topology changes by restarting and rebalancing across available nodes. [#147224](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/147224)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.26
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.26 on Github, visit [v23.2.26 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.26).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.25...v23.2.26](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.25...v23.2.26)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where using values for the cluster setting `changefeed.aggregator.flush_jitter` and the changefeed option `min_checkpoint_frequency` resulting in `changefeed.aggregator.flush_jitter * min_checkpoint_frequency < 1` would cause a panic. Jitter will now be disabled in this case. [#144423](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/144423)
- Improved the performance of `SHOW CREATE TABLE` on multi-region databases with a large numbers of objects. [#145081](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/145081)
- Fixed an internal assertion failure that could occur during operations like `ALTER TYPE` or `ALTER DATABASE... ADD REGION` when temporary tables were present. [#146200](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/146200)
- Fixed a bug that prevented `TRUNCATE` from succeeding if any indexes on the table had back-reference dependencies, such as from a view or function referencing the index. [#146322](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/146322)
- Fixed a rare corruption bug that impacts import and materialized views. [#144659](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/144659)

## v23.2.25

Release Date: April 30, 2025

### Downloads

<Note>
Experimental downloads are not qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments, whether they are for testing releases or production releases.
</Note>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.25
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.25 on Github, visit [v23.2.25 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.25).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.24...v23.2.25](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.24...v23.2.25)

### SQL language changes

- Added the `WITH IGNORE_FOREIGN_KEYS` option to `SHOW CREATE TABLE` which omits foreign key constraints from the output schema. This option is also allowed in `SHOW CREATE VIEW`, but has no effect. It cannot be combined with the `WITH REDACT` option. [#142165](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/142165)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB would encounter an internal error when decoding the gists of plans with `CALL` statements. The bug had been present since v23.2. [#143312](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143312)
- Fixed a bug that caused changefeeds to fail on startup when scanning a single key. [#143147](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143147)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a stack overflow during execution of a prepared statement that invoked a PL/pgSQL routine with a loop. The bug existed in versions v23.2.22, v24.1.15, v24.3.9, v25.1.2, v25.1.3, and pre-release versions of v25.2 prior to v25.2.0-alpha.3. [#144029](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/144029)
- Fixed a bug that could leave behind a dangling reference to a dropped role if that role had default privileges granted to itself. The bug was caused by defining privileges such as: `ALTER DEFAULT PRIVILEGES FOR ROLE self_referencing_role GRANT INSERT ON TABLES TO self_referencing_role`. [#143291](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143291)
- MVCC garbage collection is now fully subject to IO admission control. Previously, it was possible for MVCC GC to cause store overload (such as LSM inversion) when a large amount of data would become eligible for garbage collection. Should any issues arise from subjecting MVCC GC to admission control, the `kv.mvcc_gc.queue_kv_admission_control.enabled` cluster setting can be set to `false` to restore the previous behavior. [#143274](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/143274)

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.22 on Github, visit [v23.2.22 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.22).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.21...v23.2.22](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.21...v23.2.22)

### General changes

- The protected timestamp (PTS) records of running changefeeds are now updated when the set of targets changes, such as when system tables are added to the protected tables list. [#141157](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/141157)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug that could cause gateway nodes to panic when performing an `UPSERT` on a table with a `BOOL` primary key column and a partial index that used the primary key column as the predicate expression. [#141825](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/141825)
- Fixed a rare bug in which a query could fail with the error `could not find computed column expression for column in table` while dropping a virtual computed column from a table. This bug was introduced in v23.2.4. [#139874](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/139874)
- Fixed a bug that could cause `nil pointer dereference` errors when executing statements with user-defined functions (UDFs). The error could also occur when executing statements with some built-in functions, like `obj_description`. [#141666](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/141666)

### Miscellaneous

- When configuring the `sql.ttl.default_delete_rate_limit` cluster setting, a notice is displayed informing the user that the TTL rate limit is per leaseholder per table with a link to the docs. [#142831](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/142831)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.21
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.21 on Github, visit [v23.2.21 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.21).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.20...v23.2.21](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.20...v23.2.21)

### SQL language changes

- Since v23.2, table statistics histograms have been collected for non-indexed `JSONB` columns. Histograms are no longer collected for these columns if the `sql.stats.non_indexed_json_histograms.enabled` cluster setting is set to `false`. This reduces memory usage during table statistics collection, for both automatic and manual collection via `ANALYZE` and `CREATE STATISTICS`. [#140144](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140144)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where under rare circumstances draining a node could fail with `some sessions did not respond to cancellation within 1s`. [#139479](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/139479)
- Fixed a bug that prevented the `CREATE` statement for a routine from being shown in a statement bundle. This happened when the routine was created on a schema other than `public`. The bug has existed since v23.1. [#136131](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136131)
- Fixed a bounded memory leak that could previously occur when evaluating some memory-intensive queries via the vectorized engine. The leak has been present since v20.2. [#139098](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/139098)
- Previously, in changefeeds using CDC queries and the Parquet format, the output would include duplicate columns when it contained a user-defined primary key. Now, the columns are de-duplicated in Parquet changefeed messages. [#140380](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140380)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.20
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.20 on Github, visit [v23.2.20 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.20).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.19...v23.2.20](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.19...v23.2.20)

### SQL language changes

- Since v23.2, table statistics histograms have been collected for non-indexed JSON columns. Histograms are no longer collected for these columns if the `sql.stats.non_indexed_json_histograms.enabled` cluster setting is set to `false`. This reduces memory usage during table statistics collection, for both automatic and manual collection via `ANALYZE` and `CREATE STATISTICS`. [#140269](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140269)

### Operational changes

- The `changefeed.max_behind_nanos` metric now supports scoping with metrics labels. [#139241](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/139241)

### Bug fixes

- Previously, `SHOW CREATE TABLE` was showing incorrect data with regards to inverted indexes. It now shows the correct data that can be repeatedly entered back into CockroachDB to recreate the same table. [#138167](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/138167)
- Fixed a bug where querying the `pg_catalog.pg_constraint` table while the schema changer was dropping a constraint could result in a query error. [#138286](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/138286)
- Fixed a bounded memory leak that could occur when collecting table statistics on a table that had both very wide (10KiB or more) and relatively small (under 400B) `BYTES` -like values within the same row. This leak had been present since before v19.2. [#139177](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/139177)
- Fixed a bug where changefeeds using CDC queries could have duplicate columns in the Parquet output. [#140155](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140155)
- Fixed a bug that prevented the `CREATE` statement for a routine from being included in a statement bundle when the routine was created on a schema other than `public`. The bug had existed since v23.1. [#140260](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/140260)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.19
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.19 on Github, visit [v23.2.19 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.19).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.18...v23.2.19](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.18...v23.2.19)

### Security updates

- The cluster setting `server.jwt_authentication.issuers` now takes the issuers configuration value from the URI. This can be set to one of the following values:
    1. Simple string that can be parsed as a valid issuer URL. For example: `'https://accounts.google.com'`.
    2. String that can be parsed as a valid JSON array of issuer URLs list. For example: `['example.com/adfs','https://accounts.google.com']`.
    3. String that can be parsed as valid JSON and deserialized into a map of issuer URLs to corresponding JWKS URIs. In this case, the JWKS URI present in the issuer's well-known endpoint will be overridden. For example: `'{"issuer_jwks_map": {"https://accounts.google.com": "https://www.googleapis.com/oauth2/v3/certs", "example.com/adfs": "https://example.com/adfs/discovery/keys"}}'`. When `issuer_jwks_map` is set, the JWKS URI is directly used to get the key set. In all other cases when `JWKSAutoFetchEnabled` is set, the JWKS URI is obtained first from the issuer's well-known endpoint and then this endpoint is used. [#138188](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/138188)

### General changes

- In order to improve the granularity of changefeed pipeline metrics, the changefeed metrics `changefeed.admit_latency` and `changefeed.commit_latency` now have histogram buckets from `5ms` to `60m` (previously `500ms` to `5m` ). The changefeed metrics `changefeed.parallel_io_queue_nanos`, `changefeed.parallel_io_result_queue_nanos`, `changefeed.sink_batch_hist_nanos`, `changefeed.flush_hist_nanos`, and `changefeed.kafka_throttling_hist_nanos` have histogram buckets from `5ms` to `10m` (previously `500ms` to `5m` ). [#136618](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136618)
- Added support for multiple seed brokers in the new Kafka sink. [#136745](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136745)
- Added a metric `distsender.rangefeed.catchup_ranges_waiting_client_side` that counts how many rangefeeds are waiting on the client-side limiter to start performing catchup scans. [#136837](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136837)
- Added changefeed support for the `mvcc_timestamp` option with the `avro` format. If both options are specified, the Avro schema includes an `mvcc_timestamp` metadata field and emits the row's MVCC timestamp with the row data. [#136018](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136018)

### SQL language changes

- Added the `legacy_varchar_typing` session setting that reverts the changes of [#133037](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133037) that caused the change in typing behavior described in [#137837](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137837). Specifically, the `legacy_varchar_typing` session setting makes type-checking and overload resolution ignore the newly added "unpreferred" overloads. This setting defaults to `on`. [#137922](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137922)

### Operational changes

- Telemetry delivery is now considered successful even in cases where we experience a network timeout. This will prevent throttling in cases outside an operator's control. [#136477](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136477)
- When a schema change job completes, rolls back, or encounters a failure, the time taken since the job began is now logged in a structured log in the `SQL_SCHEMA` log channel. [#136952](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136952)

### Bug fixes

- `CREATE SCHEMA` now returns the correct error if the schema name is missing. [#135925](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135925)
- Fixed an issue where corrupted table statistics could cause the CockroachDB process to crash. [#136043](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136043)
- The `idle_in_session_timeout` setting now excludes the time spent waiting for schema changer jobs to complete, preventing unintended session termination during schema change operations. [#136508](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136508)
- Fixed a bug that caused the optimizer to use stale table statistics after altering an enum type used in the table. [#136832](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136832)
- CockroachDB now better respects `statement_timeout` limit on queries involving the top K sort and merge join operations. [#136650](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/136650)
- Fixed an issue where license enforcement was not consistently disabled for single-node clusters started with `start-single-node`. Now, cluster restarts correctly disable licensing. [#137009](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137009)
- Fixed a bug that caused queries against tables with user-defined types to sometimes fail with errors after restoring those tables. [#137356](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137356)
- Fixed a bug that could cause an internal error if a table with an implicit ( `rowid` ) primary key was locked from within a subquery, for example, `SELECT * FROM (SELECT * FROM foo WHERE x = 2) FOR UPDATE;`. The error could occur either under read-committed isolation, or with `optimizer_use_lock_op_for_serializable` enabled. [#137130](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137130)
- Fixed an issue where adding an existing column with the `IF NOT EXISTS` option could exit too early, skipping necessary handling of the abstract syntax tree (AST). This could lead to failure of the `ALTER` statement. [#137678](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137678)
- `CLOSE CURSOR` statements are now allowed in read-only transactions, similar to PostgreSQL. The bug has been present since at least v23.1. [#137788](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137788)
- Fixed an issue where a schema change could incorrectly cause a changefeed to fail with an assertion error like `received boundary timestamp... of type... before reaching existing boundary of type...`. [#137703](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137703)
- Internal scans are now exempt from the `sql.defaults.disallow_full_table_scans.enabled` setting, allowing index creation even when the cluster setting is enabled. [#137720](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137720)
- A new column of type `JSON` or `JSONB` that has a `UNIQUE` constraint will now be blocked from being added to a table if the cluster has not yet finalized the upgrade to v23.2. [#137864](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137864)

href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.2.18.darwin-10.9-amd64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td></tr><tr><td>ARM</td><td><a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.2.18.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz">cockroach-v23.2.18.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.2.18.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td><td><a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.2.18.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz">cockroach-sql-v23.2.18.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.2.18.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td></tr><tr><td>Windows<br/>(Experimental)</td><td>Intel</td><td><a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.2.18.windows-6.2-amd64.zip">cockroach-v23.2.18.windows-6.2-amd64.zip</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.2.18.windows-6.2-amd64.zip.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td><td><a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.2.18.windows-6.2-amd64.zip">cockroach-sql-v23.2.18.windows-6.2-amd64.zip</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.2.18.windows-6.2-amd64.zip.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td></tr></tbody></table>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.18
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.18 on Github, visit [v23.2.18 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.18).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.17...v23.2.18](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.17...v23.2.18)

### SQL language changes

- Added the `legacy_varchar_typing` session setting. When set to `on`, type-checking comparisons involving `VARCHAR` columns behave as they did in all previous versions. When set to `off`, type-checking of these comparisons is more strict and queries that previously succeeded may now error with the message `unsupported comparison operator`. These errors can be fixed by adding explicit type casts. The `legacy_varchar_typing` session setting is on by default. [#137945](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/137945)

Release Date: December 12, 2024

### Downloads

<Note>
Experimental downloads are not qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments, whether they are for testing releases or production releases.
</Note>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.17
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.17 on Github, visit [v23.2.17 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.17).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.16...v23.2.17](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.16...v23.2.17)

### Security updates

- All cluster settings that accept strings are now fully redacted when transmitted as part of Cockroach Labs' diagnostics telemetry. The payload includes a record of modified cluster settings and their values when they are not strings. If you previously applied the mitigations in Technical Advisory 133479, you can safely set the value of cluster setting `server.redact_sensitive_settings.enabled` to `false` and turn on diagnostic reporting via the `diagnostics.reporting.enabled` cluster setting without leaking sensitive cluster setting values. [#134015](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134015)

### General changes

- `COCKROACH_SKIP_ENABLING_DIAGNOSTIC_REPORTING` is no longer mentioned in the `cockroach demo` command. [#134085](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134085)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Added `system.users` to the list of system tables that changefeeds protect with protected timestamps (PTS). This table is required for CDC queries. [#134233](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134233)

### Operational changes

- Added a new cluster setting `ui.database_locality_metadata.enabled`, which allows operators to disable loading extended database and table region information in the DB Console's Databases and Table Details pages. This information can cause significant CPU load on large clusters with many ranges. Versions of this page from v24.3 onwards do not have this problem. If you require this data, you can use the `SHOW RANGES FROM {DATABASE| TABLE}` query via SQL to compute on-demand. [#134093](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134093)

### Bug fixes

- Previously, CockroachDB could encounter an internal error of the form `interface conversion: coldata.Column is` in an edge case. This is now fixed. The bug was present in versions v22.2.13 and later, v23.1.9 and later, and v23.2 and later. [#133759](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133759)
- Fixed a bug that caused incorrect `NOT NULL` constraint violation errors on `UPSERT` and `INSERT... ON CONFLICT... DO UPDATE` statements when those statements updated an existing row and a subset of columns that did not include a `NOT NULL` column of the table. This bug had been present since at least v20.1.0. [#133823](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133823)
- Fixed an unhandled error that could occur when using `REVOKE... ON SEQUENCE... FROM user` on an object that was not a sequence. [#133707](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133707)
- Addressed a panic that could occur inside `CREATE TABLE AS` that occurred if sequence builtin expressions had invalid function overloads. [#133867](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133867)
- String constants can now be compared against collated strings. [#134114](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134114)
- Previously, when executing queries with index or lookup joins when the ordering needed to be maintained, CockroachDB in some cases could get into a pathological state which would lead to increased query latency, possibly by several orders of magnitude. This bug was introduced in v22.2 and is now fixed. [#134364](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134364)
- Addressed a bug with `DROP CASCADE` that would occasionally panic with an `un-dropped backref` message on partitioned tables. [#134523](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134523)
- Reduced the duration of partitions in the gossip network when a node crashes. This eliminates false positives in the `ranges.unavailable` metric. [#134602](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134602)
- An error message is no longer returned when a non-admin user runs `DROP ROLE IF EXISTS` on a user that does not exist. [#134967](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134967)
- Fixed a bug that could cause incorrect query results when the optimizer planned a lookup join on an index containing a column of type `CHAR(N)`, `VARCHAR(N)`, `BIT(N)`, `VARBIT(N)`, or `DECIMAL(M, N)`, and the query held that column constant to a single value (e.g., with an equality filter). [#135113](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135113)
- Fixed an unhandled error that would occur if `DROP SCHEMA` was executed on the `public` schema of the `system` database, or on an internal schema like `pg_catalog` or `information_schema`. [#135196](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135196)
- Fixed a bug that caused incorrect evaluation of some binary expressions involving `CHAR(N)` values and untyped string literals with trailing whitespace characters. For example, the expression `'f'::CHAR = 'f '` now correctly evaluates to `true`. [#135691](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135691)

### Performance improvements

- CockroachDB now avoids loading unnecessary file blocks shortly after a rebalance in a rare case. [#134526](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134526) [#135303](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135303) [#135577](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135577)
- Reduced the write-amplification impact of rebalances by splitting snapshot sstable files into smaller ones before ingesting them into Pebble. [#134526](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134526) [#135303](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135303) [#135577](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135577)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.16
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.16 on Github, visit [v23.2.16 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.16).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.15...v23.2.16](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.15...v23.2.16)

### General changes

- Changed the license `cockroach` is distributed under to the new CockroachDB Software License (CSL). [#131705](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131705) [#131927](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131927) [#131933](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131933) [#131981](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131981) [#131988](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131988) [#131994](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131994) [#131992](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131992) [#132000](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132000) [#132001](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132001) [#131999](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131999) [#132053](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132053) [#132803](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132803) [#132781](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132781)
- The cluster setting `diagnostics.reporting.enabled` is now ignored if the cluster has a Enterprise Trial or Enterprise Free license, or if the reporting job is unable to load any license at all. [#132461](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132461)
- Added the sink error metric ( `changefeed.sink_errors` ) and expanded the reporting of the internal retries metric ( `changefeed.internal_retry_message_count` ) to all changefeed sinks that perform internal retries. [#132569](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132569)
- Allowed access to DB console APIs via JWT, which can be supplied as a Bearer token in the Authorization header. [#133240](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133240)

### DB Console changes

- DB Console will reflect any throttling behavior from the cluster due to an expired license or missing telemetry data. Enterprise licenses are not affected. [#131859](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131859)
- Due to the inaccuracy of the **Range Count** column on the **Databases** page, and the cost incurred to fetch the correct range count for every database in a cluster, this data will no longer be visible. This data is still available via a `SHOW RANGES` query. [#133271](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133271)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed an error that could happen if an aggregate function was used as the value in a `SET` command. [#131958](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131958)
- Added automated clean-up/validation for dropped roles inside of default privileges. [#132169](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132169)
- Fixed a bug that could cause `RESTORE` to hang after encountering transient errors from the storage layer. [#132260](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132260)
- Fixed a bug that caused incorrect evaluation of `CASE`, `COALESCE`, and `IF` expressions with branches producing fixed-width string-like types, such as `CHAR`. In addition, the `BPCHAR` type has been fixed so that it no longer incorrectly imposes a length limit of `1`. [#130898](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130898)
- Fixed a bug that could lead to incorrect results in rare cases. The bug requires a `JOIN` between two tables, with an equality between columns with equivalent, but not identical types (e.g., `OID` and `REGCLASS` ). In addition, the `JOIN` must lookup an index that includes a computed column that references one of the equivalent columns. This bug has existed since before v23.1. [#132510](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132510)
- Fixed a bug that could lead to incorrect results in rare cases. The bug requires a lookup join into a table with a computed index column, where the computed column expression is composite sensitive. A composite sensitive expression can compare differently if supplied non-identical, but equivalent input values (e.g. `2.0::DECIMAL` vs `2.00::DECIMAL` ). This bug has existed since before v23.1. [#132510](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132510)
- Fixed a bug where a span stats request on a mixed-version cluster resulted in an NPE. [#132683](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132683)
- The `franz-go` library has been updated to fix a potential deadlock on changefeed restarts. [#132784](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132784)
- Fixed an issue where changefeeds would fail to update protected timestamp records in the face of retryable errors. [#132774](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132774)
- Fixed a bug that could result in changefeeds using CDC queries failing due to a system table being garbage collected. [#131655](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131655)
- Fixed a rare bug in which an update of a primary key column that is also the only column in a separate column family can sometimes fail to update the primary index. This bug has existed since v22.2. Requirements to hit the bug are:
    1. A table with multiple column families.
    2. A column family containing a single primary key column.
    3. That column family is not the first column family.
    4. That column family existed before its column was in the primary key.
    5. That column must be of type `FLOAT4/8`, `DECIMAL`, `JSON`, collated string type, or array.
    6. An update that changes that column from a composite value to a non-composite value. [#132123](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132123)
- The `proretset` column of the `pg_catalog.pg_proc` table is now properly set to `true` for set-returning builtin functions. [#132874](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132874)
- Fixed a bug in the query optimizer that could cause CockroachDB nodes to crash in rare cases. The bug could occur when a query contains a filter in the form `col IN (elem0, elem1,..., elemN)` only when `N` is very large, e.g., 1.6+ million, and when `col` exists in a hash-sharded index or, exists in a table with an indexed, computed column dependent on `col`. [#133066](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133066)
- Users with the `admin` role can now run `ALTER DEFAULT PRIVILEGES FOR target_role...` on any `target_role`. Previously, this could result in a privilege error, which is incorrect as admins are allowed to perform any operation. [#133069](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133069)
- `REASSIGN OWNED BY` will now transfer ownership of the `public` schema. Previously, it would always skip over the `public` schema even if it was owned by the target role. [#133069](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133069)
- Added a timer for inner changefeed sink client flushes. Fixed a bug where timers were not correctly registered with the metric system. [#133255](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/133255)
- Fixed an error that could be caused by using an `AS OF SYSTEM TIME` expression that references a user-defined (or unknown) type name. These kinds of expressions are invalid, but previously the error was not handled properly. This will now return the correct error message. [#132453](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132453)
- Fixed a bug where backup schedules could advance a protected timestamp too early, which caused incremental backups to fail. [#131389](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131389)

### Performance improvements

- Performance has been improved during periodic polling of table history when the `schema_locked` table storage parameter is not enabled. [#132240](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/132240)
- Reduced the write-amplification impact of rebalances by splitting snapshot SSTable files into smaller ones before ingesting them into Pebble. [#134526](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/134526)

## v23.2.15

Release Date: November 15, 2024

### Downloads

<Note>
Experimental downloads are not qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments, whether they are for testing releases or production releases.
</Note>

<table><thead><tr><th>Operating System</th><th>Architecture</th><th>Full executable</th><th>SQL-only executable</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td rowspan="2">Linux</td><td>Intel</td><td><a ### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.15
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.15 on Github, visit [v23.2.15 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.15).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.14...v23.2.15](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.14...v23.2.15)

### Performance improvements

- Reduced the write-amplification impact of rebalances by splitting snapshot `sstable` files before ingesting them into Pebble. [#135123](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/135123)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.13
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.13 on Github, visit [v23.2.13 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.13).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.12...v23.2.13](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.12...v23.2.13)

### Enterprise edition changes

- The description for the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `changefeed.sink_io_workers` now lists all <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks" data-versioned="true">changefeed sinks</a> that support the setting. [#130372](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130372)
- Network metrics have been added for the following <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks" data-versioned="true">changefeed sinks</a>:
- Added two network metrics, `changefeed.network.bytes_in` and `changefeed.network.bytes_out`. These metrics track the number of bytes sent by individual <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a> to the following sinks:
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks#kafka" data-versioned="true">Kafka sinks</a>. If child metrics are enabled, the metric will have a `kafka` label.
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks#webhook-sink" data-versioned="true">Webhook sinks</a>. If child metrics are enabled, the metric will have a `webhook` label.
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks#google-cloud-pub-sub" data-versioned="true">Pub/Sub sinks</a>. If child metrics are enabled, the metric will have a `pubsub` label.
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-for" data-versioned="true">SQL sink</a>. If child metrics are enabled, the metric will have a `sql` label.

        [#130664](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130664)
- The new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metric</a> `changefeed.total_ranges` allows observation of the number of ranges that are watched by a changefeed aggregator. It uses the same polling interval as `changefeed.lagging_ranges`, which is controlled by the changefeed option `lagging_ranges_polling_interval`. [#130984](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130984)
- The following groups of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metrics</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging" data-versioned="true">logs</a> have been renamed to include the buffer they are associated with. The previous metrics are still maintained for backward compatibility.
    - `changefeed.buffer_entries.*`
    - `changefeed.buffer_entries_mem.*`
    - `changefeed.buffer_pushback_nanos.*`

        [#131417](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131417)
- Added timers and corresponding [metrics](https://www.cockroachlabs.com/docs/v24.2/metrics.html for key parts of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> pipeline to help debug issues with feeds. The `changefeed.stage.{stage}.latency` metrics now emit latency histograms for each stage. The metrics respect the changefeed `scope` label to debug a specific feed. [#131428](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131428)

### Operational changes

- The new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metric</a> `ranges.decommissioning` shows the number of ranges with a replica on a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/node-shutdown" data-versioned="true">decommissioning node</a>. [#130251](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130251)
- The following new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metrics</a> show the number of RPC TCP connections established to remote nodes:
    - `rpc.connection.connected`: the number of gRPC TCP level connections established to remote nodes.
    - `rpc.client.bytes.egress`: the number of TCP bytes sent over gRPC on connections initiated by the cluster.
    - `rpc.client.bytes.ingress`: the number of TCP bytes received over gRPC on connections initiated by the cluster.

        [#130521](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130521)
- Added a new configuration parameter, `server.cidr_mapping_url`, which maps IPv4 CIDR blocks to arbitrary tag names. [#130528](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130528)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metrics</a> `sql.bytesin` and `sql.bytesout` are now aggregate metrics if child metrics are enabled. [#130528](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130528)
- The following new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metrics</a> track the number of bytes sent by an individual <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> to each sink:
    - `changefeed.network.bytes_in`
    - `changefeed.network.bytes_out`

        [#130664](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130664)
- You can now set the log format for the `STDERR` changefeed sink using the `format` field in the `stderr` sink section of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging" data-versioned="true">logging</a> configuration. [#131533](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131533)

### DB Console changes

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> now shows a notification if the cluster has no Enterprise license set. Refer to [upcoming license changes](https://www.cockroachlabs.com/enterprise-license-update) for more information. [#130425](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130425)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where the command `SHOW CLUSTER SETTING FOR VIRTUAL CLUSTER` would erroneously return `NULL` for some settings. [#128782](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128782)
- Fixed a bug where a node could fail to start with the error `could not insert session...: unexpected value` if an ambiguous result error occurred while inserting data into the `sqlliveness` table. [#130343](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130343)
- Fixed a bug that could prevent <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upgrade-cockroach-version" data-versioned="true">upgrade finalization</a> due to the upgrade pre-condition for repairing descriptor corruption. [#130519](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130519)
- Fixed a rare bug where a lease transfer could lead to a `side-transport update saw closed timestamp regression` panic. The bug could occur when a node was overloaded and failing to heartbeat its node liveness record. [#130790](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130790)
- Fixed a bug that could result in the erroneous log message `expiration of liveness record... is not greater than expiration of the previous lease... after liveness heartbeat`. [#130790](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130790)
- Fixed a bug where queries that are not initiated within a SQL session could fail to respect a statement timeout, including <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">background jobs</a>, queries issued by the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> that perform introspection, and the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroachcloud/sql-shell" data-versioned="true">CockroachDB Cloud SQL Shell</a>. [#130790](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130790)
- Fixed a bug where a connection could be incorrectly dropped if the client was attempting to change a schema at the same time that the same schema's objects were being dropped. [#130964][#130964]
- Fixed a bug that could cause the following error to be logged when executing a query under <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/read-committed" data-versioned="true">READ COMMITTED</a> isolation if it involved a table with `NOT NULL` virtual columns: `internal error: Non-nullable column...`. [#131065](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131065)
- Fixed a potential memory leak in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a> that use a cloud storage sink. The memory leak could occur if both of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> `changefeed.fast_gzip.enabled` and `changefeed.cloudstorage.async_flush.enabled` were `true` **and** if the changefeed received an error while attempting to write to the sink. [#130614](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130614)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.2.6, where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-statistics" data-versioned="true">statistics</a> forecasting could predict a result of zero rows for a downward-trending statistic when `sql.stats.forecasts.max_decrease` is `false`. The setting is now enabled (set to `1/3` by default). [#131128](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131128)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.1 that can cause incorrect results in the following scenario:
    1. The query contains a correlated subquery.
    2. The correlated subquery has a `GroupBy` or `DistinctOn` operator with an outer-column reference in its input.
    3. The correlated subquery is in the input of a `SELECT` or `JOIN` clause that has a filter that sets the outer-column reference equal to an inner column that is in the input of the grouping operator.
    4. The set of grouping columns does not include the replacement column explicitly.

        [#130988](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130988)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cloud-storage-authentication" data-versioned="true">AWS S3 and HTTP client configurations</a> were not considered when implicit authentication was used. [#131201](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/131201)
- Fixed a bug that could prevent a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> from resuming from a prolonged paused state. [#130919](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130919)

## v23.2.12

Release Date: September 25, 2024

### Downloads

<Note>
Experimental downloads are not qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments, whether they are for testing releases or production releases.
</Note>

<table><thead><tr><th>Operating System</th><th>Architecture</th><th>Full executable</th><th>SQL-only executable</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td rowspan="2">Linux</td><td>Intel</td><td><a ### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.12
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.12 on Github, visit [v23.2.12 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.12).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.11...v23.2.12](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.11...v23.2.12)

### Enterprise edition changes

Added a `changefeed.protect_timestamp.lag` metric, which controls how much the changefeed <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/protect-changefeed-data" data-versioned="true">protected timestamp (PTS)</a> should lag behind the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/how-does-an-enterprise-changefeed-work" data-versioned="true">high-water mark</a>. A changefeed now only updates its PTS if `changefeed.protect_timestamp.lag` has passed between the last PTS and the changefeed high-water mark. [#129685](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129685) - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs#show-changefeed-jobs" data-versioned="true">`SHOW CHANGEFEED JOB`</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs#show-changefeed-jobs" data-versioned="true">`SHOW CHANGEFEED JOBS`</a>, and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">`SHOW JOBS`</a> no longer expose user sensitive information like `client_key`. [#122681](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122681)

### SQL language changes

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> `plan_cache_mode=force_generic_plan` can now be used to force prepared statements to use a query plan that is <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimized</a> once and reused in future executions without re-optimization, as long as the plan does not become stale due to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">schema changes</a> or a collection of new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-statistics" data-versioned="true">table statistics</a>. The setting takes effect during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sql-grammar#execute_stmt" data-versioned="true">`EXECUTE`</a> commands. <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/explain-analyze" data-versioned="true">`EXPLAIN ANALYZE`</a> now includes a `plan type` field. If a generic query plan is optimized for the current execution, the `plan type` will be `generic, re-optimized`. If a generic query plan is reused for the current execution without performing optimization, the `plan type` will be `generic, reused`. Otherwise, the `plan type` will be `custom`. [#128100](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128100)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> `plan_cache_mode=auto` can now be used to instruct the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">cost-based optimizer</a> to automatically determine whether to use "custom" or "generic" query plans for the execution of a prepared statement. Custom query plans are optimized on every execution, while generic plans are optimized once and reused on future executions as-is. Generic query plans are beneficial in cases where query optimization contributes significant overhead to the total cost of executing a query. [#128100](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128100)

### Operational changes

- There are now structured logging events that report connection breakage during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/node-shutdown" data-versioned="true">node shutdown</a>. Previously, these logs existed but were unstructured. These logs appear in the `OPS` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging-overview#logging-channels" data-versioned="true">logging channel</a>. There are two new events:
    - The `node_shutdown_connection_timeout` event is logged after the timeout defined by the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-server-shutdown-connection-wait" data-versioned="true">cluster setting `server.shutdown.connections.timeout`</a> transpires, if there are still open SQL connections.
    - The `node_shutdown_transaction_timeout` event is logged after the timeout defined by the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-server-shutdown-query-wait" data-versioned="true">cluster setting `server.shutdown.transactions.timeout` transpires</a>, if there are still open <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transactions" data-versioned="true">transactions</a> on those SQL connections. [#128710](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128710)
- Added the `ranges.decommissioning` metric, representing the number of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-range" data-versioned="true">ranges</a> which have a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-replica" data-versioned="true">replica</a> on a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-node#decommission-nodes" data-versioned="true">decommissioning node</a>. [#130413](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130413)
- Added three new network tracking metrics:
    - `rpc.connection.connected` is the number of rRPC TCP-level connections established to remote nodes.
    - `rpc.client.bytes.egress` is the number of TCP bytes sent via gRPC on connections we initiated.
    - `rpc.client.bytes.ingress` is the number of TCP bytes received via gRPC on connections we initiated. [cockroachdb/cockroach#130712](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130712)
- Added a new configuration parameter `server.cidr_mapping_url`, which maps IPv4 CIDR blocks to arbitrary tag names. [#130712](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130712)
- Modified metrics `sql.bytesin` and `sql.bytesout` to be aggregation metrics If the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-server-child-metrics-enabled" data-versioned="true">`server.child_metrics.enabled`</a> cluster setting is enabled. [#130712](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130712)
- Added two network metrics, `changefeed.network.bytes_in` and `changefeed.network.bytes_out`. These metrics track the number of bytes sent by individual <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-and-configure-changefeeds" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a> to the following sinks:
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks#kafka" data-versioned="true">Kafka sinks</a>. If the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-server-child-metrics-enabled" data-versioned="true">`server.child_metrics.enabled`</a> cluster setting is enabled, the metric will have a `kafka` label.
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks#webhook-sink" data-versioned="true">Webhook sinks</a>. If the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-server-child-metrics-enabled" data-versioned="true">`server.child_metrics.enabled`</a> cluster setting is enabled, the metric will have a `webhook` label.
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks#google-cloud-pub-sub" data-versioned="true">Pub/Sub sinks</a>. If the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-server-child-metrics-enabled" data-versioned="true">`server.child_metrics.enabled`</a> cluster setting is enabled, the metric will have a `pubsub` label.
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-for" data-versioned="true">SQL sink</a>. If the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-server-child-metrics-enabled" data-versioned="true">`server.child_metrics.enabled`</a> cluster setting is enabled, the metric will have a `sql` label. [#130712](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130712)

### DB Console changes

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview-dashboard" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> time-series graphs now have hover behavior that focuses on individual lines and shows values under the mouse pointer. [cockroachdb/cockroach#128864](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128864)
- Users with the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#viewactivity" data-versioned="true">`VIEWACTIVITY` privilege</a> can download <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/explain-analyze" data-versioned="true">statement bundles</a> from <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a>. [#129502](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129502)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> now displays an alert message when the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/licensing-faqs#monitor-for-license-expiry" data-versioned="true">license is expired</a> or if there are fewer than 15 days left before the license expires. [#130509](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130509)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> will now show a notification alerting customers without an Enterprise license to [upcoming license changes](https://www.cockroachlabs.com/enterprise-license-update) with a link to more information. [#130509](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130509)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where declarative and legacy <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">schema changes</a> were incorrectly allowed to be executed concurrently, which could lead to failing or hung schema change jobs. [#128838](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128838)
- Fixed a bug that caused errors like `ERROR: column 'crdb_internal_idx_expr' does not exist` when accessing a table with an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/expression-indexes" data-versioned="true">expression index</a> where the expression evaluates to an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/enum" data-versioned="true">`ENUM`</a> type, e.g., `CREATE INDEX ON t ((col::an_enum))`. [#129092](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129092)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">Function</a> input parameters can no longer have the `VOID` type. [#129281](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129281)
- Internally issued queries that are not initiated within a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-sessions" data-versioned="true">SQL session</a> no longer respect a statement timeout. This includes: <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">background jobs</a>, queries issued by the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> that perform introspection, and the Cloud <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroachcloud/sql-shell" data-versioned="true">SQL shell</a>. [#129517](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129517)
- Fixed a bug where the `schema_locked` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/with-storage-parameter" data-versioned="true">storage parameter</a> did not prevent a table from being referenced by a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/foreign-key" data-versioned="true">foreign key</a>. [#129753](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129753)
- Users with the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#viewactivity" data-versioned="true">`VIEWACTIVITY` SQL privilege</a> can now request, view, and cancel <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/explain-analyze" data-versioned="true">statement bundles</a> in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a>. [#129803](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129803)
- Fixed a bug where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#epoch-based-leases-table-data" data-versioned="true">lease transfer</a> could lead to a panic with the message `side-transport update saw closed timestamp regression`. The bug could occur when a node was overloaded and failing to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-setup-troubleshooting#node-liveness-issues" data-versioned="true">heartbeat its node liveness record</a>. [#129808](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129808)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging-overview" data-versioned="true">log message</a> `expiration of liveness record... is not greater than expiration of the previous lease... after liveness heartbeat` is no longer generated. [#129808](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129808)
- Fixed a bug where the `require_explicit_primary_keys` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> would prevent all <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-table" data-versioned="true">`CREATE TABLE`</a> statements from working. [#129906](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129906)
- Fixed a slow-building memory leak when using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/gssapi_authentication" data-versioned="true">Kerberos authentication</a>. [#130317](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130317)
- Fixed a potential memory leak in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-examples#create-a-changefeed-connected-to-a-cloud-storage-sink" data-versioned="true">changefeeds using a cloud storage sink</a>. The memory leak could occur if both <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-changefeed-fast-gzip-enabled" data-versioned="true">`changefeed.fast_gzip.enabled`</a> and `changefeed.cloudstorage.async_flush.enabled` were `true`, and the changefeed received an error while attempting to write to the cloud storage sink. [#130624](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130624)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.11
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.11 on Github, visit [v23.2.11 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.11).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.10...v23.2.11](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.10...v23.2.11)

### Bug fixes

- Internally issued queries that are not initiated within a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-sessions" data-versioned="true">SQL session</a> no longer respect a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables#statement-timeout" data-versioned="true">statement timeout</a>. This includes: background <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">jobs</a>, queries issued by the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> that perform introspection, and the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroachcloud/sql-shell" data-versioned="true">Cloud SQL shell</a>. [#130525](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130525)
- Fixed a rare bug where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#leases" data-versioned="true">lease transfer</a> could lead to a `side-transport update saw closed timestamp regression` panic. The bug could occur when a node was <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overload-dashboard" data-versioned="true">overloaded</a> and failing to heartbeat its <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-setup-troubleshooting#node-liveness-issues" data-versioned="true">node liveness</a> record. [#130523](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130523)
- Resolved a concerning <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging-overview" data-versioned="true">log</a> message: `expiration of liveness record... is not greater than expiration of the previous lease... after liveness heartbeat`. This message is no longer possible. [#130523](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130523)

## v23.2.10

Release Date: August 29, 2024

### Downloads

<Note>
Experimental downloads are not qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments, whether they are for testing releases or production releases.
</Note>

<table><thead><tr><th>Operating System</th><th>Architecture</th><th>Full executable</th><th>SQL-only executable</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td rowspan="2">Linux</td><td>Intel</td><td><a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.2.10.linux-amd64.tgz">cockroach-v23.2.10.linux-amd64.tgz</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.2.10.linux-amd64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td><td><a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.2.10.linux-amd64.tgz">cockroach-sql-v23.2.10.linux-amd64.tgz</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.2.10.linux-amd64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td></tr><tr><td>ARM</td><td><a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.2.10.linux-arm64.tgz">cockroach-v23.2.10.linux-arm64.tgz</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.2.10.linux-arm64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2">Mac<br/>(Experimental)</td><td>Intel</td><td><a
