### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.10
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.10 on Github, visit [v23.2.10 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.10).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.9...v23.2.10](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.9...v23.2.10)

### Security updates

- URLs in the following SQL statements are now sanitized of any secrets, such as keys or passwords, before being written to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-logs#redact-logs" data-versioned="true">unredacted logs</a>:
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-backup-schedule" data-versioned="true">`ALTER BACKUP SCHEDULE`</a>
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-backup" data-versioned="true">`ALTER BACKUP`</a>
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-changefeed#set-options-on-a-changefeed" data-versioned="true">`ALTER CHANGEFEED SET sink`</a>
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/backup" data-versioned="true">`BACKUP`</a>
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/copy" data-versioned="true">`COPY`</a>
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed" data-versioned="true">`CREATE CHANGEFEED`</a>
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-external-connection" data-versioned="true">`CREATE EXTERNAL CONNECTION`</a>
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-schedule-for-backup" data-versioned="true">`CREATE SCHEDULE FOR BACKUP`</a>
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-schedule-for-changefeed" data-versioned="true">`CREATE SCHEDULE FOR CHANGEFEED`</a>
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/export" data-versioned="true">`EXPORT`</a>
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/import-into" data-versioned="true">`IMPORT INTO`</a>
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a>
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-backup" data-versioned="true">`SHOW BACKUPS`</a>
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-backup" data-versioned="true">`SHOW BACKUP`</a> [#127509](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127509)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks#kafka" data-versioned="true">Kafka sink</a> utilizing the `franz-go` library and our own `batching_sink` behind a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> ( `changefeed.new_kafka_sink_enabled`, disabled by default). [#128048](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128048)
- The v2 Kafka and Google Cloud Pub/Sub <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks" data-versioned="true">changefeed sinks</a> now display notices indicating the topics they will emit to. [#128459](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128459)

### SQL language changes

- Added the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-sql-auth-grant-option-for-owner-enabled" data-versioned="true">`sql.auth.grant_option_for_owner.enabled` cluster setting</a>. The default value is `true`, which results in behavior that matches the existing behavior of CockroachDB. When set to `false`, then the `GRANT OPTION` is not implcitly given to the owner of an object. The object owner still implicitly has all privileges on the object, just not the ability to grant them to other users. [#126958](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126958)
- Fixed a bug where the `DISCARD` statement was disallowed when the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables#default-transaction-read-only" data-versioned="true">`default_transaction_read_only`</a> session setting was set to `on`. [#127548](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127548)

### DB Console changes

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">**Databases** and **Tables** pages</a> in the DB Console now show a loading state while loading information for databases and tables, including size and range counts. [#127709](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127709)
- On the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">**Databases** page</a> in the DB Console, table names will no longer appear with quotes around the schema and table name. [#127765](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127765)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug causing gateway nodes to crash while executing <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/insert" data-versioned="true">`INSERT`</a> statements in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/table-localities#regional-by-row-tables" data-versioned="true">`REGIONAL BY ROW`</a> tables. This bug had been present since v23.2. [#127276](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127276)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-type#drop-a-value-in-a-user-defined-type" data-versioned="true">dropping `ENUM` values</a> that were referenced by <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/expression-indexes" data-versioned="true">index expressions</a> could fail with an error. [#127453](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127453)
- Fixed a bug that caused a memory leak when executing SQL statements with comments, e.g., <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-clause" data-versioned="true">`SELECT /* comment */ 1;`</a>. Memory owned by a SQL session would continue to grow as these types of statements were executed. The memory would only be released when closing the SQL session. This bug had been present since v23.1. [#127758](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127758)
- Fixed a memory leak that could occur when specifying a non-existent <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-virtualization-overview" data-versioned="true">virtual cluster</a> name in the connection string. [#128104](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128104)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-index" data-versioned="true">`CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS`</a> would not correctly short-circuit if the given index already existed. [#128312](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128312)
- Fixed a bug in overly eager syntax validation, which did not allow the `DESCENDING` clause for non-terminal columns of an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/inverted-indexes" data-versioned="true">inverted index</a>. Only the last column of an inverted index should be prevented from being `DESCENDING`, and this is now properly checked. [#128312](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128312)
- Fixed a bug where an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes" data-versioned="true">index</a> could store a column in the primary index if that column had a mixed-case name. [#128312](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128312)
- Fixed small memory leaks that would occur during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed" data-versioned="true">changefeed creation</a>. [#128048](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128048)
- Setting or dropping a default value on a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/computed-columns" data-versioned="true">computed column</a> is now blocked -- even for null defaults. Previously, setting or dropping a default value on a computed column was a no-op; now there will be an error message. [#128467](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128467)
- Fixed a bug that could cause spurious user permission errors when multiple databases shared a common schema with a routine referencing a table. The bug had existed since <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">user-defined functions</a> were introduced in v22.2. [#126413](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126413)
- Fixed a bug where a hash-sharded constraint could not be created if it referred to columns that had a backslash in the name. [#128676](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128676)
- Fixed a bug where `TYPEDESC SCHEMA CHANGE` jobs could end up retrying forever if the descriptor targeted by them was already dropped. [#128461](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128461)
- Fixed a bug in which the output of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/explain" data-versioned="true">`EXPLAIN (OPT, REDACT)`</a> for various `CREATE` statements was not redacted. This bug had existed since <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/explain#parameters" data-versioned="true">`EXPLAIN (REDACT)`</a> was introduced in v23.1 and affects the following statements:
    - `EXPLAIN (OPT, REDACT) CREATE TABLE`
    - `EXPLAIN (OPT, REDACT) CREATE VIEW`
    - `EXPLAIN (OPT, REDACT) CREATE FUNCTION` [#128488](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128488)

### Contributors

This release includes 80 merged PRs by 28 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.9
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.9 on Github, visit [v23.2.9 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.9).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.8...v23.2.9](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.8...v23.2.9)

### SQL language changes

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/explain-analyze" data-versioned="true">`EXPLAIN ANALYZE`</a> statements are now supported when executed via Cloud Console <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroachcloud/sql-shell" data-versioned="true">SQL shell</a>. [#125562](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125562)
- Added the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-sql-auth-grant-option-inheritance-enabled" data-versioned="true">`sql.auth.grant_option_inheritance.enabled` cluster setting</a>. The default value is `true`, which maintains consistency with CockroachDB's previous behavior: users granted a privilege with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/grant" data-versioned="true">`WITH GRANT OPTION`</a> can in turn grant that privilege to others. When `sql.auth.grant_option_inheritance.enabled` is set to `false`, the `GRANT OPTION` is not inherited through role membership, thereby preventing descendant roles from granting the privilege to others. However, the privilege itself continues to be inherited through role membership. [#126298](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126298)

### Operational changes

- `crdb_internal.cluster_execution_insights.txt` and `crdb_internal.cluster_txn_execution_insights.txt` have been removed from the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-zip" data-versioned="true">debug zip</a>. These files contained cluster-wide insights for statements and transactions. Users can still rely on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-zip#files" data-versioned="true">per-node execution</a> insights in `crdb_internal.node_execution_insights.txt` and `crdb_internal.node_txn_execution_insights.txt`. [#125804](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125804)
- Some debugging-only information about physical plans is no longer collected in the `system.job_info` table for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a>, because it has the potential to grow very large. [#126097](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126097)
- For the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging#telemetry" data-versioned="true">TELEMETRY channel</a>, TCL <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/eventlog#sampled_query" data-versioned="true">`sampled_query`</a> events will now be sampled at the rate specified by the setting <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-sql-telemetry-query-sampling-max-event-frequency" data-versioned="true">`sql.telemetry.query_sampling.max_event_frequency`</a>, which is already used to limit the rate of sampling DML statements. [#126728](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126728)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.2.0 in which CockroachDB would hit an internal error when evaluating <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/insert" data-versioned="true">`INSERT`s</a> into <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#set-the-table-locality-to-regional-by-row" data-versioned="true">`REGIONAL BY ROW`</a> tables where the source was a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/selection-queries#values-clause" data-versioned="true">`VALUES`</a> clause with a single row and at least one boolean expression. [#125504](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125504) [#126839](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126839)
- Fixed a bug where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-role" data-versioned="true">`DROP ROLE`</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-user" data-versioned="true">`DROP USER`</a> command could leave references behind inside types, which could prevent subsequent <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-grants" data-versioned="true">`SHOW GRANTS`</a> commands from working. [#125806](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125806)
- Fixed a bug that could lead to descriptors having privileges to roles that no longer exist. Added an automated clean up for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-role" data-versioned="true">dropped roles</a> inside descriptors. [#125806](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125806)
- Fixed a bug where a change to a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type" data-versioned="true">user-defined type (UDT)</a> could cause queries against tables using that type to fail with an error message like: `histogram.go:694: span must be fully contained in the bucket`. The change to the user-defined type could occur either directly from an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-type" data-versioned="true">`ALTER TYPE`</a> statement or indirectly from an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-database#add-region" data-versioned="true">`ALTER DATABASE... ADD REGION`</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-database#drop-region" data-versioned="true">`ALTER DATABASE... DROP REGION`</a> statement, which implicitly modifies the `crdb_internal_region` UDT. This bug had existed since UDTs were introduced in v20.2. [#125806](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125806)
- Fixed a bug in which constant `LIKE` patterns containing certain sequences of backslashes did not become constrained scans. This bug has been present since v21.1.13 when support for building constrained scans from `LIKE` patterns containing backslashes was added. [#125538](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125538)
- Fixed a bug introduced in alpha versions of v23.1 where calling a routine could result in an unexpected `function... does not exist` error. The bug is triggered when the routine is called twice using the exact same SQL query, and either: (a) the routine has polymorphic arguments, or: (b) between the two calls, the routine is replaced by a routine with the same name and different parameters. [#123518](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123518)
- Fixed the statistics estimation code in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> so it does not use the empty histograms produced if <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#control-histogram-collection" data-versioned="true">histogram collection</a> has been disabled during stats collection due to excessive memory utilization. Now the optimizer will rely on distinct counts instead of the empty histograms and should produce better plans as a result. This bug has existed since v22.1. [#126156](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126156)
- Fixed a bug in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-tsdump" data-versioned="true">`cockroach debug tsdump`</a> where the command fails when a custom SQL port is used and the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-tsdump#flags" data-versioned="true">`--format=raw`</a> flag is provided. [#126184](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126184)
- Fixed a bug where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">user-defined function (UDF)</a> that shared a name with a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators#built-in-functions" data-versioned="true">built-in function</a> would not be resolved, even if the UDF had higher precedence according to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sql-name-resolution#search-path" data-versioned="true">`search_path`</a> variable. [#126295](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126295)
- Fixed a bug that caused <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">background jobs</a> to incorrectly respect a statement timeout. [#126819](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126819)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-database#drop-region" data-versioned="true">`ALTER DATABASE... DROP REGION`</a> could fail if any tables under the given database have <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/expression-indexes" data-versioned="true">indexes on expressions</a>. [#126598](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126598)
- Fixed a bug when <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">restoring</a> a database with a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type#create-a-composite-data-type" data-versioned="true">composite type</a>. [#126841](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126841)
- Fixed a bug when inputting `public` role as user name for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators#compatibility-functions" data-versioned="true">built-in compatibility functions</a>, such as `has_database_privilege` and `has_schema_privilege`. [#126852](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126852)
- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">Database page</a> could crash if range information is not available. [#127091](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127091)
- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB could incorrectly evaluate an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/null-handling#nulls-and-simple-comparisons" data-versioned="true">`IS NOT NULL`</a> filter if it was applied to non- `NULL` tuples that had `NULL` elements, such as `(1, NULL)` or `(NULL, NULL)`. This bug has existed since v20.2. [#126937](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126937)
- In the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview-dashboard#events-panel" data-versioned="true">DB Console event log</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-role" data-versioned="true">`ALTER ROLE`</a> events now display correctly even when no <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-role#role-options" data-versioned="true">role options</a> are included in the `ALTER ROLE` statement. [#126565](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126565)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-table" data-versioned="true">`CREATE TABLE`</a> with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/expression-indexes" data-versioned="true">index expressions</a> could hit undefined column errors on <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transactions#transaction-retries" data-versioned="true">transaction retries</a>. [#126201](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126201)

### Performance improvements

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">Schema changes</a> that cause a data backfill, such as adding a non-nullable column or changing the primary key, will now split and scatter the temporary indexes used to perform the change. This reduces the chance of causing a write hotspot that can slow down foreground traffic. [#126691](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126691)

### Contributors

This release includes 100 merged PRs by 33 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.8
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.8 on Github, visit [v23.2.8 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.8).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.7...v23.2.8](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.7...v23.2.8)

### Performance improvements

- Updated the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer" data-versioned="true">replica allocator</a> with a small performance win for very large clusters. [#126918](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull#126918)
- Updated the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/distribution-layer" data-versioned="true">gossip layer</a> to avoid unnecessary mutex contention. [#126919](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126919), [#126920](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126920)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where the `disallow_full_table_scans` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables#disallow-full-table-scans" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> was not working for tables with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/hash-sharded-indexes" data-versioned="true">hash-sharded indexes</a>. [#126700](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126700)

### Contributors

This release includes 5 merged PRs by 4 authors.

### Downloads

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.7
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.7 on Github, visit [v23.2.7 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.7).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.6...v23.2.7](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.6...v23.2.7)

### Enterprise edition changes

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">Changefeeds</a> can use the bulk oracle for planning, which distributes work evenly across all <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/reads-and-writes-overview#replica" data-versioned="true">replicas</a> in the locality filter, including followers if enabled. Set the `changefeed.random_replica_selection.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> to `true` to enable this planning behavior. To use the previous bin-packing oracle, set the cluster setting `changefeed.random_replica_selection.enabled` to `false`. [#124925](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124925)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-changefeed" data-versioned="true">`ALTER CHANGEFEED`</a> no longer removes the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cdc-queries" data-versioned="true">CDC query</a> when modifying changefeed properties. [#125437](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125437)

### SQL language changes

- Precision is no longer limited when encoding `geo` data types to JSON. [#124535](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124535)
- When the new `optimizer_push_offset_into_index_join` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> is enabled, the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> attempts to produce more efficient query plans by attempting to push offset expressions into index join expressions to produce more efficient query plans. [#124492](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124492)

### General changes

- CockroachDB v23.2.7 and subsequent v23.2 releases are eligible for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/release-support-policy#support-types" data-versioned="true">long term support (LTS)</a>.

### Operational changes

- Improved metrics related to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-storage-dashboard#capacity-metrics" data-versioned="true">disk usage</a> reporting for volumes that dynamically change their size over time. [#125107](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125107)

### Security changes

- Improved the automated cleanup when dropping roles inside descriptors. [#124665](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124665)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where a range with a replication factor of `1` to be scaled up to a replication factor of `2`. [#124487](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124487)
- Fixed a bug that could cause leases to thrash between nodes when perturbed with a replication factor of `1`. [#124487](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124487)
- Fixed a bug where, when the `ttl_row_stats_poll_interval` storage parameter is non-zero, the job to update row statistics for a table with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl" data-versioned="true">row-level TTL</a> enabled could be blocked from completing by the queries issued to update the row statistics. Now, if the job completes, these queries are cancelled, and the `jobs.row_level_ttl.total_rows` and `jobs.row_level_ttl.total_expired_rows` metrics will report 0 if the job finishes before the queries to update the row statistics complete. [#124626](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124626)
- Fixed a bug where the `results_buffer_size` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> could not be configured using the `options` query parameter in the connection string, but only as a top-level query parameter. This variable cannot be changed by using the `SET` command after the session begins. [#124774](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124774)
- Fixed a bug where dropping a role or user could leave references behind inside types. This in turn could prevent the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-grants" data-versioned="true">`SHOW GRANTS`</a> command from working correctly. [#124644](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124644)
- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#alter-primary-key" data-versioned="true">`ALTER TABLE... ALTER PRIMARY KEY`</a> command could hang for a table if its indexes are referred to by views or functions using the `force syntax` syntax. [#124569](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124569)
- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-types" data-versioned="true">`SHOW TYPES`</a> command omitted user-defined composite types. This bug was introduced in v23.1. [#124816](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124816)
- Fixed a bug where if a column name that contains UTF-8 characters is referenced in the `STORING()` clause of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-index" data-versioned="true">`CREATE INDEX`</a> command, the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">declarative schema changer</a> cannot detect whether the column is already handled by an existing index. [#125211](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125211)
- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">declarative schema changer</a> erroneously includes virtual columns that are referenced in the `STORING()` clause of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-index" data-versioned="true">`CREATE INDEX`</a> command. [#125211](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125211)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v20.2, where a change to a user-defined type could cause queries against tables using that type to fail with the error like `histogram.go: span must be fully contained in the bucket`. This bug could occur if the change was from an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table" data-versioned="true">`ALTER TABLE`</a> command or from an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-database" data-versioned="true">`ALTER DATABASE... ADD REGION`</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-database" data-versioned="true">`ALTER DATABASE... DROP REGION`</a> command, which implicitly change the non-public `crdb_internal_region` type. [#124853](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124853)
- Fixed a bug where telemetry logs could emit the same statement fingerprint ID for different SQL statements. [#125043](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125043)
- Fixed a bug where adding a column with a default value of an empty array could fail. [#125326](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125326)
- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">declarative schema changer</a> could erroneously succeed despite a violation of an `ALTER TABLE... ADD CONSTRAINT UNIQUE` constraint. Now such a violation results in an error message with the error code `42601`. [#125418](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125418)
- Fixed a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-and-configure-changefeeds" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> panic in v24.1, v23.2, and v23.1 when the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `changefeed.aggregator.flush_jitter` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> is configured and a changefeed's <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed#min-checkpoint-frequency" data-versioned="true">`min_checkpoint_frequency`</a> option is set to zero. [#125469](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125469)
- Fixed a bug where the public schema was erroneously created with its owner set to the `admin` role instead of the database owner. Ownership of the public schema can be altered after the schema is created. [#125535](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125535)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.2.0 where inserting rows into a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/table-localities#regional-by-row-tables" data-versioned="true">`REGIONAL BY ROW` table</a> could cause an internal error if the source was a `VALUES` clause with a single row and at least one boolean expression. [#126208](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126208)

### Performance improvements

- The optimizer now generates more efficient query plans for some queries with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/limit-offset#offset" data-versioned="true">`OFFSET`</a> clauses. [#124492](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124492)

### Contributors

This release includes 77 merged PRs by 30 authors.

## v23.2.6

href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.2.6.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz">cockroach-v23.2.6.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.2.6.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td><td><a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.2.6.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz">cockroach-sql-v23.2.6.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.2.6.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td></tr><tr><td>Windows<br/>(Experimental)</td><td>Intel</td><td><a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.2.6.windows-6.2-amd64.zip">cockroach-v23.2.6.windows-6.2-amd64.zip</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.2.6.windows-6.2-amd64.zip.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td><td><a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.2.6.windows-6.2-amd64.zip">cockroach-sql-v23.2.6.windows-6.2-amd64.zip</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.2.6.windows-6.2-amd64.zip.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td></tr></tbody></table>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.6
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.6 on Github, visit [v23.2.6 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.6).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.5...v23.2.6](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.5...v23.2.6)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Fixed a bug that was present since v22.2 where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a> with long-running <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed#initial-scan" data-versioned="true">initial scans</a> might incorrectly restore checkpoint job progress and drop events during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-messages#duplicate-messages" data-versioned="true">changefeed restarts</a> due to transient errors or node restarts. The bug was most likely to occur in clusters with the following contributing factors:
    - The `changefeed.shutdown_checkpoint.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> was enabled.
    - The cluster settings `changefeed.frontier_checkpoint_frequency` and `low changefeed.frontier_highwater_lag_checkpoint_threshold` were set low, which resulted in the initial scan taking many multiples of the configured frequency to complete.
    - There were multiple target tables with significant differences in row counts in one changefeed.
    - The changefeed target tables were large with many ranges.
    - The initial scan took a long time to complete (an hour or longer). [#123966](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123966)

### SQL language changes

- Updated the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-grants" data-versioned="true">`SHOW GRANTS`</a> responses to display the `object_type` and `object_name`, which has replaced the `relation_name` column. [#122822](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122822)
- Added <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-external-connection" data-versioned="true">external connection</a> granted privileges to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-grants" data-versioned="true">`SHOW GRANTS`</a> command. [#122822](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122822)
- Introduced three new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> for controlling table statistics forecasting:
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">`sql.stats.forecasts.min_observations`</a> is the minimum number of observed statistics required to produce a forecast.
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">`sql.stats.forecasts.min_goodness_of_fit`</a> is the minimum R² (goodness of fit) measurement required from all predictive models to use a forecast.
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">`sql.stats.forecasts.max_decrease`</a> is the most a prediction can decrease, expressed as the minimum ratio of the prediction to the lowest prior observation. [#122458](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122458)
- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> `optimizer_use_improved_multi_column_selectivity_estimate`, which if enabled, causes the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> to use an improved selectivity estimate for multi-column predicates. This setting will default to `true` on v24.2 and later, and `false` on earlier versions. [#123100](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123100)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> can now plan constrained scans over partial indexes in more cases, particularly on <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/partial-indexes" data-versioned="true">partial indexes</a> with predicates referencing <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/computed-columns" data-versioned="true">virtual computed columns</a>. [#123469](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123469)
- The row-level TTL setting <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl" data-versioned="true">`ttl_delete_rate_limit`</a> is now set to `100` by default, which sets the rate limit for deleting expired rows to `100`. [#124353](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124353)

### Operational changes

- Two new metrics track the status of the SQL Activity Update job, which pre-aggregates top K information within the SQL statistics subsytem and writes the results to `system.statement_activity` and `system.transaction_activity`:
    - `sql.stats.activity.updates.successful`: Number of successful updates made by the SQL activity updater job.
    - `sql.stats.activity.update.latency`: The latency of updates made by the SQL activity updater job. Includes failed update attempts. [#123960](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123960)
- Added a new counter <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metric</a>, `sql.stats.flush.done_signals.ignored`, that tracks the number of times the SQL activity update job has ignored the signal that indicates that a flush has completed. This metric may indicate that the SQL activity update job is taking longer than expected to complete. [#123960](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123960)
- Added a new counter <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metric</a>, `sql.stats.activity.updates.failed`, to measure the number of update attempts made by the SQL activity update job that failed with errors. The SQL activity update job is used to pre-aggregate top K information within the SQL stats subsystem and write the results to `system.statement_activity` and `system.transaction_activity`. [#123960](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123960)
- Added a new counter <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metric</a>, `sql.stats.flush.fingerprint.count`, that tracks the number of unique statement and transaction fingerprints included in the SQL stats flush. [#123960](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123960)
- Added the `sql.pgwire.pipeline.count` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metric</a>, which measures how many wire protocol commands have been received by the server, but have not yet started processing. This metric will only grow if clients are using the [pipeline mode](https://www.postgresql.org/docs/current/libpq-pipeline-mode) of the PostgreSQL wire protocol. [#124260](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124260)
- The `client_authentication_ok` and `client_session_end` events are now logged to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging-use-cases#sessions" data-versioned="true">`SESSIONS` log channel</a> unconditionally. Previously, these would only be logged if the `server.auth_log.sql_sessions.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> was set to `true`. All other `SESSIONS` log messages are still only logged if `server.auth_log.sql_sessions.enabled` or `server.auth_log.sql_connections.enabled` are set to `true`. To not show `client_authentication_ok` and `client_session_end` events, disable the `SESSIONS` log channel entirely. [#124374](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124374)

### DB Console changes

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">**Database**</a> details and **Table** details pages now display the correct stats in the **Table Stats Last Updated**. [#122815](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122815)
- Viewing the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page#active-executions-view" data-versioned="true">**SQL Activity**</a> sorted by `% of Runtime` now correctly sorts entries by the runtime amount. [#123901](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123901)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/authentication#client-authentication" data-versioned="true">client certificate authentication</a> combined with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sso-sql#identity-map-configuration" data-versioned="true">identity maps</a> ( `server.identity_map.configuration` ) did not work. For the feature to work correctly, the client must specify a valid database user in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/connection-parameters" data-versioned="true">connection string</a>. [#122749](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122749)
- Fixed a bug where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/sql-layer#query-execution" data-versioned="true">row-based execution engine</a> could drop a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/limit-offset" data-versioned="true">`LIMIT`</a> clause when there was an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/order-by" data-versioned="true">`ORDER BY`</a> clause, and the ordering was partially provided by an input operator. For example, this bug could occur with an ordering such as `ORDER BY a, b` when the scanned index was only ordered on column `a`. The impact of this bug was that more rows may have been returned than specified by the `LIMIT` clause. This bug is only present when not using the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/sql-layer#vectorized-query-execution" data-versioned="true">vectorized execution engine</a>; that is, when running with `SET vectorize = off;`. This bug has existed since CockroachDB v22.1. [#122836](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122836)
- Fixed a bug in the DB Console's <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-custom-chart-debug-page" data-versioned="true">**Custom Chart**</a> tool where store-level metrics were displayed only for the first store ID associated with the node. Now data is displayed for all stores present on a node, and a single time series is shown for each store, rather than an aggregated value for all of the node's stores. This allows finer-grained monitoring of store-level metrics. [#122703](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122703)
- Fixed a bug where privileges granted for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-external-connection" data-versioned="true">external connections</a> were incorrectly showing up in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-system-grants" data-versioned="true">`SHOW SYSTEM GRANTS`</a>, but were not useful because there was no associated object name. The privileges no longer appear in `SHOW SYSTEM GRANTS`. Instead, the `SHOW GRANTS ON EXTERNAL CONNECTION` statement should be used. [#122905](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122905)
- Statistics forecasts of zero rows can cause suboptimal <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">query plans</a>. Forecasting will now avoid predicting zero rows for most downward-trending statistics. [#122458](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122458)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.2 that could cause a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/plpgsql" data-versioned="true">PL/pgSQL</a> routine to return incorrect results when the routine included:
    - At least one parameter.
    - An `IF` statement with one leak-proof branch and one branch with side effects. [#120742](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120742)
- Fixed a bug that could result in an internal error when attempting to create a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/plpgsql" data-versioned="true">PL/pgSQL</a> routine using the (currently unsupported) `%ROWTYPE` syntax for a variable declaration. [#123010](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123010)
- Fixed a bug where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a> of a backup that itself contained a table created by the `RESTORE` of a table with an in-progress <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/import-into" data-versioned="true">`IMPORT INTO`</a> would fail to restore all rows. [#120543](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120543)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.2 that could cause a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/plpgsql" data-versioned="true">PL/pgSQL</a> variable assignment to not be executed if the variable was never referenced after the assignment. [#123116](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123116)
- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB could run into an `attempting to append refresh spans after the tracked timestamp has moved forward` internal error in some edge cases. The bug had been present since v22.2. [#123150](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123150)
- A <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">job</a> will now log rather than fail if it reports an out-of-bound progress fraction. [#122964](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122964)
- Fixed a bug that would occur when <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-type" data-versioned="true">`ALTER TYPE... DROP VALUE`</a> is followed by <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-schema" data-versioned="true">`DROP SCHEMA CASCADE...`</a> in the same transaction. Previously, the `ALTER TYPE` schema change would get queued up to run at commit time, but by that point, the type may have already been removed, so the commit could fail. [#123576](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123576)
- Fixed a bug that could lead to descriptors with self references that pointed to incorrect descriptor IDs. Now, tables that see the error `invalid inbound foreign key... origin table ID should be` or `invalid outbound foreign key... reference table ID should be` will automatically repair post deserialization. [#123681](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123681)
- Fixed a bug where a failed <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">restore</a> job could leave the system in a state where re-attempting the restore was not possible without manual intervention. [#123463](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123463)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page#index-recommendations" data-versioned="true">Index recommendations</a> in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> will now function properly for indexes on tables or columns whose names contain quotation marks or whitespace. For example: `CREATE INDEX ON "my table" ("my col");`. [#122119](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122119)
- Fixed a crash introduced in v23.2.5 that could occur when planning <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#enable-and-disable-automatic-statistics-collection-for-clusters" data-versioned="true">statistics collection</a> on a table with a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/computed-columns" data-versioned="true">virtual computed column</a> using a user-defined type when the newly introduced <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `sql.stats.virtual_computed_columns.enabled` is set to `true`. (The setting was introduced in v23.2.4 and set to `false` by default.) [#124080](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124080)
- Added automated clean up and validation for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-role" data-versioned="true">dropped roles</a> inside descriptors. [#124670](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124670)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-role" data-versioned="true">`DROP ROLE`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-user" data-versioned="true">`DROP USER`</a> could leave references behind inside types, which could prevent <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-grants" data-versioned="true">`SHOW GRANTS`</a> from working. [#124668](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124668)
- Fixed a bug where a change to a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type" data-versioned="true">user-defined type</a> could cause queries against tables using that type to fail with the error `histogram.go:694: span must be fully contained in the bucket`. The change to the user-defined type could come directly from an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-type" data-versioned="true">`ALTER TYPE`</a> statement, or indirectly from an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-database#add-region" data-versioned="true">`ALTER DATABASE ADD REGION`</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-database#drop-region" data-versioned="true">`DROP REGION`</a> statement (which implicitly change the `crdb_internal_region` type). This was present since user-defined types were introduced in v20.2. [#124854](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124854)

### Performance improvements

- More efficient <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">query plans</a> are now generated for queries with text similarity filters, for example, `text_col % 'foobar'`. These plans are generated if the `optimizer_use_trigram_similarity_optimization` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> is enabled. It is disabled by default. [#122753](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122753)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> now costs <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-clause#eliminate-duplicate-rows" data-versioned="true">`distinct-on`</a> operators more accurately. It may produce more efficient query plans in some cases. [#122844](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122844)
- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> `optimizer_use_improved_zigzag_join_costing`. When enabled and when the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `enable_zigzag_join` is also enabled, the cost of zigzag joins is updated such that a zigzag join will be chosen over a scan only if it produces fewer rows than a scan. [#123100](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123100)
- Improved the selectivity estimation of multi-column filters when the multi-column distinct count is high. This prevents the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> from choosing a bad query plan due to over-estimating the selectivity of a multi-column predicate. [#123100](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123100)
- Improved the efficiency of error handling in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/vectorized-execution" data-versioned="true">vectorized execution engine</a> to reduce the CPU overhead of statement timeout handling and reduce the potential for more statement timeouts. [#123502](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123502)

### Contributors

This release includes 115 merged PRs by 32 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.5
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.5 on Github, visit [v23.2.5 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.5).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.4...v23.2.5](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.4...v23.2.5)

### SQL language changes

- The new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-sql-stats-virtual-computed-columns-enabled" data-versioned="true">`sql.stats.virtual_computed_columns.enabled`</a> enables collection of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics" data-versioned="true">table statistics</a> on virtual <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/computed-columns" data-versioned="true">computed columns</a>. [#120923](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120923)
- The new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> `optimizer_use_virtual_computed_column_stats` configures the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> to consider table statistics on virtual computed columns. [#121179](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121179)
- The new `FORCE_INVERTED_INDEX` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes#selection" data-versioned="true">hint</a> configures the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> to prefer a query plan scan over any inverted index of the hinted table. If no such query plan can be generated, an error is logged. [#122300](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122300)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> can now plan constrained scans over <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/partial-indexes" data-versioned="true">partial indexes</a> in more cases, particularly on partial indexes with predicates referencing virtual <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-sql-stats-virtual-computed-columns-enabled" data-versioned="true">computed columns</a>. [#123408](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123408)

### Operational changes

- A minimum <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#raft" data-versioned="true">Raft</a> scheduler concurrency is now enforced per <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start#storage" data-versioned="true">store</a> so that a node with many stores does not spread workers too thinly. This avoids high scheduler latency across <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/glossary#replica" data-versioned="true">replicas</a> on a store when load is imbalanced. [#120798](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120798)
- A <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> optimization to reduce duplicates during aggregator restarts has been disabled due to poor performance. [#123596](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123596)

### DB Console changes

- The **Commit Latency** chart in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-cdc-dashboard" data-versioned="true">Changefeed Dashboard</a> now aggregates by max instead of by sum for multi-node changefeeds. This more accurately reflects the amount of time for events to be acknowledged by the downstream sink. [#121235](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121235)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a slow memory leak when opening many new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/connect-to-the-database" data-versioned="true">connections</a>. This bug was introduced in v22.2.9 and v23.1.0. [#121055](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121055)
- Fixed a bug that occurred when using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table" data-versioned="true">`ALTER TABLE`</a> to drop and re-add a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/check" data-versioned="true">`CHECK` constraint</a> with the same name. [#121055](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121055)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-sequence" data-versioned="true">Sequence</a> options `MINVALUE` and `MAXVALUE` automatically adjust to new types bounds. This mirrors the behavior of PostgreSQL. [#121309](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121309)
- Fixed a bug that could prevent timeseries graphs shown on the DB Console SQL Activity <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">Statement Details</a> page from rendering correctly when specifying a custom time range. [#121383](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121383)
- Fixed a bug present since at least v21.1 that could lead to incorrect evaluation of an `IN` expression with:
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/int" data-versioned="true">`INT2` or `INT4`</a> type on the left side, and
    - Values on the right side that are outside of the range of the left side.

        [#121953](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121953)
- Fixed a leak in reported memory usage (not the actual memory usage) by the internal memory accounting system, the limit for which is configured via the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start#flags" data-versioned="true">`--max-sql-memory`</a> flag when a long-running sessions issues hundreds of thousands or more <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transactions" data-versioned="true">transactions</a>. This reporting bug could cause `root: memory budget exceeded` errors for other queries. The bug was introduced in v23.1.17 and v23.2.3. [#121950](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121950)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.2.4 that could prevent collection of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics" data-versioned="true">table statistics</a> on tables that have on virtual <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/computed-columns" data-versioned="true">computed columns</a> of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type" data-versioned="true">user-defined type</a> when the newly-introduced <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-sql-stats-virtual-computed-columns-enabled" data-versioned="true">`sql.stats.virtual_computed_columns.enabled`</a> is set to `true` (defaults to `false`). The setting was introduced in v23.2.4 and is disabled by default. [#122319](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122319)
- Fixed a bug where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/grant" data-versioned="true">`GRANT... ON ALL TABLES`</a> statement could fail if a sequence existed that did not support the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#privileges" data-versioned="true">privilege</a> being granted. [#122034](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122034)
- Fixed an existing bug where an unused value cannot be dropped from an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/enum" data-versioned="true">`ENUM`</a> if the`ENUM` itself is referenced by a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">user-defined function</a>. A value can now be dropped from an`ENUM` as long as the value itself is not being referenced by any other data element, including a user-defined function. [#121237](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121237)

### Contributors

This release includes 79 merged PRs by 33 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.4
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.4 on Github, visit [v23.2.4 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.4).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.3...v23.2.4](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.3...v23.2.4)

### SQL language changes

- Mutation statements such as <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/update" data-versioned="true">`UPDATE`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/delete" data-versioned="true">`DELETE`</a> as well as locking statements such as <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-for-update" data-versioned="true">`SELECT FOR UPDATE`</a> are not allowed in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-transaction#parameters" data-versioned="true">read-only transactions</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-transaction#parameters" data-versioned="true">`AS OF SYSTEM TIME` transactions</a>. Previously, a bug existed where mutation statements and locking statements in implicit single-statement transactions using AS OF SYSTEM TIME were allowed. [#120158](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120158)
- The new cluster setting <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-sql-stats-virtual-computed-columns-enabled" data-versioned="true">`sql.stats.virtual_computed_columns.enabled`</a>, when enabled, allows the collection of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-statistics" data-versioned="true">table statistics</a> on <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/computed-columns" data-versioned="true">virtual computed columns</a>. [#120933](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120933)
- The new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> `optimizer_use_virtual_computed_column_stats`, when enabled, configures the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">cost-based optimizer</a> to use <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-statistics" data-versioned="true">table statistics</a> on <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/computed-columns" data-versioned="true">virtual computed columns</a>. [#121329](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121329)

### DB Console changes

- Fixed an issue where clusters with multiple <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start#store" data-versioned="true">stores</a> per node could list inaccurate region and node information on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page#databases" data-versioned="true">**Databases** page</a>. [#120212](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120212)
- Users will no longer see <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/views" data-versioned="true">views</a> displayed on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page#databases" data-versioned="true">**Databases** page</a>. Previously views would be listed with no information, only displaying errors. [#120214](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120214)

### Bug fixes

- Previously, on long-running <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-sessions" data-versioned="true">sessions</a> that issue many (hundreds of thousands or more) <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transactions" data-versioned="true">transactions</a>, CockroachDB's internal memory accounting system, the limit for which is configured via the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start#general" data-versioned="true">`--max-sql-memory` flag</a> ) could leak. This bug, in turn, could result in the error message `"root: memory budget exceeded"` for other queries. The bug was present in v23.2.3 and is now fixed. [#121875](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121875)
- Previously, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#set-locality" data-versioned="true">altering a table's locality</a> from <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#set-the-table-locality-to-regional-by-row" data-versioned="true">`REGIONAL BY ROW`</a> to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#regional-by-table" data-versioned="true">`REGIONAL BY TABLE`</a> could cause <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#leases" data-versioned="true">leaseholders</a> to never move to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-database#set-primary-region" data-versioned="true">database's primary region</a>. This is now fixed. [#118794](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118794)
- A user with the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#privileges" data-versioned="true">`VIEWACTIVITYREDACTED` privilege</a> can no longer see constants inside of queries that originate from other users in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-sessions#response" data-versioned="true">`SHOW SESSIONS` result</a>. Previously, this redaction did not occur. [#119884](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119884)
- Previously, the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-statements" data-versioned="true">`SHOW STATEMENTS`</a> and the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-statements#aliases" data-versioned="true">`SHOW QUERIES`</a> commands incorrectly required the user to have the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#privileges" data-versioned="true">`VIEWACTIVITY` or `VIEWACTIVITYREDACTED` privilege</a>. However, a user always should be able to view their own queries, even without these privileges. This is now fixed. [#119884](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119884)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a> on certain <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/backup" data-versioned="true">`BACKUP`s</a> would open a very large number of connections to the backup storage provider. [#119883](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119883)
- Fixed a bug that occurred when using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table" data-versioned="true">`ALTER TABLE`</a> to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#drop-constraint" data-versioned="true">drop</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#add-constraint" data-versioned="true">add</a> back a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/check" data-versioned="true">`CHECK` constraint</a> with the same name. [#120075](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120075)
- Fixed a bug in which it was possible to set <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> `transaction_read_only` to `false` during an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-transaction#parameters" data-versioned="true">`AS OF SYSTEM TIME` transaction</a>. [#120158](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120158)
- Fixed a bug where some files were not closed when inspecting <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/backup-architecture#metadata-writing-phase" data-versioned="true">backup metadata</a> during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/backup" data-versioned="true">`BACKUP`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a>. [#119635](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119635)
- Fixed an intermittent page crash on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroachcloud/insights-page#schema-insights-tab" data-versioned="true">**Schema Insights**</a> view. [#120210](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120210)

### Contributors

This release includes 65 merged PRs by 37 authors
