### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.3
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.3 on Github, visit [v23.2.3 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.3).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.2...v23.2.3](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.2...v23.2.3)

### Security updates

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> `session` cookie is now marked `HttpOnly` to prevent it from being read by any Javascript code. Cookies are also marked `Secure` for the browser when the cluster is running in secure mode. [#119259](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119259)
- Clusters using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sso-sql" data-versioned="true">Cluster Single Sign-on (SSO) with JSON web tokens (JWTs)</a> can now optionally fetch signing keys from configured issuers instead of configuring static signing keys for each issuer. When the new cluster setting `server.jwt_authentication.jwks_auto_fetch.enabled` is set to `true`, signing keys are automatically fetched from the issuer using metadata published in its OpenID configuration. In this case, static signing keys in `server.jwt_authentication.jwks` are ignored. When automatic fetching is enabled, there may be a slight increase in network latency for each JWT authentication request, proportional to the latency between the cluster and the issuer's endpoint. [#119768](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119768)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Fixed a bug where creating a changefeed with the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed#format" data-versioned="true">`format='avro'`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed#diff-opt" data-versioned="true">`diff`</a> options that targeted tables with a `DECIMAL(n)` column (i.e., zero-scale `DECIMAL` column) would cause a panic. [#118847](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118847)

### SQL language changes

- Changed the `sql.index_recommendation.drop_unused_duration` cluster setting to `public` so that it is documented on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">Cluster Settings</a> page. [#118764](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118764)
- Added the `server.max_open_transactions_per_gateway` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a>. When set to a non-negative value, non-admin users cannot execute a query if the number of transactions open on the current gateway node is already at the configured limit. [#118933](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118933)
- Out-of-process SQL servers will now start exporting a new `sql.aggregated_livebytes` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metric</a>. This metric gets updated once every 60 seconds by default, and its update interval can be configured via the `tenant_global_metrics_exporter_interval` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a>. [#119371](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119371)
- Added support for index hints with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/insert" data-versioned="true">`INSERT`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upsert" data-versioned="true">`UPSERT`</a> statements. This allows `INSERT... ON CONFLICT` and `UPSERT` queries to use index hints in the same way they are already supported for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/update" data-versioned="true">`UPDATE`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/delete" data-versioned="true">`DELETE`</a> statements. [#119601](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119601)

### Operational changes

- Expanded the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-zip" data-versioned="true">`--include-range-info`</a> flag to include problem ranges. This flag still defaults to `true`. [#119234](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119234)
- In unredacted <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-zip" data-versioned="true">debug zips</a>, the `crdb_internal.transaction_contention_events` table file has two new columns:
    - `waiting_stmt_query`: the query of the waiting statement.
    - `blocking_txn_queries_unordered`: the unordered list of the blocking transaction's queries. [#118831](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118831)

### Command-line changes

- Updated the SQL shell help URL to point to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-sql" data-versioned="true">`cockroach sql`</a> page. [#118994](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118994)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-tsdump" data-versioned="true">`cockroach debug tsdump`</a> creates a `tsdump.yaml` file. The `tsdump` raw format automatically creates the YAML file in the default location `/tmp/tsdump.yaml`. Added a new flag `--yaml` that allows users to specify the path to create `tsdump.yaml` instead of using the default location. For example, `cockroach debug tsdump --host <host>:<port> \ --format raw --yaml=/some_path/tsdump.yaml > /some_path/tsdump.gob`. [#117741](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117741)

### DB Console changes

- Fixed a bug where a warning about the need to refresh data would remain displayed on the Active Executions view of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page#active-executions-view" data-versioned="true">Statements</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-transactions-page#active-executions-view" data-versioned="true">Transactions</a> pages despite enabling **Auto Refresh**. [#118703](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118703)
- Updated the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">Statement Details page</a> to always show the entire selected period, instead of just the period that had data. [#118805](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118805)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overload-dashboard" data-versioned="true">Overload dashboard</a> now includes two additional graphs:
    - **Elastic CPU Utilization**: displays the CPU utilization by elastic work, compared to the limit set for elastic work.
    - **Elastic CPU Exhausted Duration Per Second**: displays the duration of CPU exhaustion by elastic work, in microseconds. [#118896](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118896)
- The **Full Table/Index Scans** chart in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-sql-dashboard" data-versioned="true">SQL Metrics dashboard</a> now shows the non-negative derivative of the number of full scans tracked. [#118860](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118860)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> could omit events in rare cases, logging the error `cdc ux violation: detected timestamp... that is less or equal to the local frontier`. This could happen in the following scenario:
    1. A <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-and-configure-changefeeds#enable-rangefeeds" data-versioned="true">rangefeed</a> runs on a follower <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/glossary#cockroachdb-architecture-terms" data-versioned="true">replica</a> that lags significantly behind the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/glossary#cockroachdb-architecture-terms" data-versioned="true">leaseholder</a>.
    2. A transaction commits and removes its transaction record before its <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/transaction-layer#writing" data-versioned="true">intent</a> resolution is applied on the follower.
    3. The follower's <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/transaction-layer#closed-timestamps" data-versioned="true">closed timestamp</a> has advanced past the transaction commit timestamp.
    4. The rangefeed attempts to push the transaction to a new timestamp (at least 10 seconds after the transaction began).
    5. This may cause the rangefeed to prematurely emit a checkpoint before emitting writes at lower timestamps, which in turn may cause the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/how-does-an-enterprise-changefeed-work" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> to drop these events entirely, never emitting them. [#118413](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118413)
- Decommissioning replicas that are part of a mis-replicated range will no longer get stuck on a rebalance operation that was falsely determined to be unsafe. This bug was introduced in v23.1.0. [#118343](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118343)
- CockroachDB will no longer spam the logs with `unable to get CPU capacity` errors every 10 seconds when running outside of a CPU cgroup. [#118672](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118672)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics" data-versioned="true">`AUTO CREATE STATS`</a> jobs could previously lead to growth in an internal system table resulting in slower job-system related queries. [#118942](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118942)
- Fixed a bug that caused an inscrutable error when a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-sequence" data-versioned="true">sequence</a> name allocated by `SERIAL` conflicted with an existing type name. [#118947](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118947)
- Fixed an internal error with a message like: `LeafTxn... incompatible with locking request` that occurs when performing an update under <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/read-committed" data-versioned="true">`READ COMMITTED` isolation</a> that cascades to a table with multiple other foreign keys. [#118931](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118931)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#alter-primary-key" data-versioned="true">`ALTER PRIMARY KEY`</a> could fail with an error `non-nullable column <x> with no value! Index scanned..` when validating recreated <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/schema-design-indexes" data-versioned="true">secondary indexes</a>. [#118974](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118974)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/comment-on" data-versioned="true">`COMMENT ON`</a> statements could fail with an `unexpected value` error if multiple `COMMENT` statements were running concurrently. [#119020](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119020)
- Previously, in certain cases, using virtual tables such as `crdb_internal.system_jobs` could result in the internal error `attempting to append refresh spans after the tracked timestamp has moved forward`. This is now fixed. The bug was introduced in CockroachDB v23.1. [#119184](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119184)
- Fixed a bug where operations on the `crdb_internal.leases` table could cause a node to become unavailable due to a deadlock in the leasing subsystem. [#119341](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119341)
- Fixed a bug where rangefeed resolved timestamps could get stuck, continually emitting the log message `pushing old intents failed: range barrier failed, range split`, typically following a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/distribution-layer#range-merges" data-versioned="true">range merge</a>. [#119541](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119541)
- Fixed a bug where running a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> that targets a table with a user-defined type column and with the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed#envelope" data-versioned="true">`envelope` option</a> set to any value other than `wrapped` would cause a node panic due to a nil dereference. [#119738](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119738)
- Fixed a rare panic that could happen during a `pg_dump` import that contains a function that has a subquery in one of its arguments, like `SELECT addgeometrycolumn(...)`. Now, attempting to import a `pg_dump` with such a function results in an expected error. [#118612](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118612)
- Users with the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges" data-versioned="true">VIEWACTIVITY</a> privilege can now request statement bundles using `crdb_internal.request_statement_bundle` or through the DB Console <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges" data-versioned="true">SQL Activity</a> page. [#118809](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118809)
- Fixed a bug in changefeed <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeed-sinks#webhook-sink" data-versioned="true">webhook sinks</a> where the HTTP request body may not be initialized on retries, resulting in the error `http: ContentLength=... with Body length 0`. [#119496](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119496)
- Fixed a bug that caused internal errors when executing an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/export" data-versioned="true">`EXPORT`</a> statement. [#119711](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119711)
- Fixed a bug that could lead to schema changes with a large number of descriptors doing full table scans on `system.leases`. [#119464](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119464)
- Fixed a bug where rangefeed resolved timestamps could get stuck, continually emitting the log message `pushing old intents failed: range barrier failed, range split`, typically following a range merge. This bug was introduced in v23.2.1. [#119702](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119702)
- Fixed a bug that occurred when using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table" data-versioned="true">`ALTER TABLE`</a> to drop and re-add a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/check" data-versioned="true">`CHECK`</a> constraint with the same name. [#120076](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120076)
- Fixed a bug that caused a slow memory leak that can accumulate when opening many new connections. The bug was present in v22.2.9+ and v23.1+ versions. [#120245](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120245)

### Contributors

This release includes 118 merged PRs by 42 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.2
```

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.2 on Github, visit [v23.2.2 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.2).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.1...v23.2.2](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.1...v23.2.2)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-and-configure-changefeeds#enable-rangefeeds" data-versioned="true">rangefeed</a> resolved timestamps could get stuck, continually emitting the log message `pushing old intents failed: range barrier failed, range split`, typically following a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/distribution-layer#range-merges" data-versioned="true">range merge</a>. This bug was introduced in v23.2.1. [#119558](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119558)

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.1
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.1 on Github, visit [v23.2.1 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.1).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.0...v23.2.1](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.0...v23.2.1)

### Security updates

- Introduced the `server.redact_sensitive_settings.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a>, which is false by default. If set to `true`, then the values of the following settings will be redacted when accessed through `SHOW` commands or other introspection interfaces. In the future, any other sensitive cluster settings that are added will be redacted as well. Users who have the `MODIFYCLUSTERSETTING` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#managing-privileges" data-versioned="true">privilege</a> can always view the unredacted settings. [#117729](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117729)
    - `server.oidc_authentication.client_id`
    - `server.oidc_authentication.client_secret`
- If the `server.redact_sensitive_settings.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> is set to `true`, then the `MANAGEVIRTUALCLUSTER` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#managing-privileges" data-versioned="true">privilege</a> is required to view the values of the per-virtual-cluster overrides for sensitive cluster settings. [#117729](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117729)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> `session` cookie is now marked `HttpOnly` to prevent it from being read by any JavaScript code. [#119249](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119249)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> cookies are marked `Secure` for the browser when the cluster is running in secure mode. [#119249](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119249)

### General changes

- Updated Go version to 1.21.3. [#115339](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115339)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">SQL function</a> `fips_ready`, which can be used to verify the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/fips" data-versioned="true">FIPS</a> readiness of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/life-of-a-distributed-transaction#gateway" data-versioned="true">gateway node</a>. [#115202](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115202)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/physical-cluster-replication-overview" data-versioned="true">Physical Cluster Replication (PCR)</a> now retries for approximately 3 minutes before failing. This is increased from 20 µs. [#116402](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116402)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-and-configure-changefeeds" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a> that targeted schema-locked tables could fail due to a very old highwater timestamp being incorrectly persisted. [#117961](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117961)
- Fixed a bug where creating a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-and-configure-changefeeds" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> that targeted tables with a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/decimal" data-versioned="true">`DECIMAL(n)`</a> column (i.e., zero-scale `DECIMAL` column), `format='avro'`, and `diff` would cause a panic. [#118895](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118895)

### SQL language changes

- Added the `sql.ttl.default_select_rate_limit` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> and the `ttl_select_rate_limit` table <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl#ttl-storage-parameters" data-versioned="true">storage parameter</a> to set the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl" data-versioned="true">TTL</a> select rate limit. This sets the number of records per table per second per node that can be selected by the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl#view-scheduled-ttl-jobs" data-versioned="true">TTL job</a>. [#115801](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115801)
- Fixed a bug in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/plpgsql" data-versioned="true">PL/pgSQL</a> where altering the name of a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-sequence" data-versioned="true">sequence</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type" data-versioned="true">user-defined type (UDT)</a> that was used in a PL/pgSQL <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">function</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/stored-procedures" data-versioned="true">procedure</a> could break them. This bug was only present in v23.2 alpha and beta releases. [#116419](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116419)
- Added support for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/import-into" data-versioned="true">`IMPORT INTO`</a> on a table that has columns typed as <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/array" data-versioned="true">arrays</a> of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type" data-versioned="true">user-defined types</a> (like <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/enum" data-versioned="true">enums</a> ). Tables that use multiple user-defined types with the same name but different <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-schema" data-versioned="true">schemas</a> are still unsupported. [#116359](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116359)
- The new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-for-update" data-versioned="true">`SELECT FOR UPDATE`</a> implementation used under <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/read-committed" data-versioned="true">Read Committed isolation</a> (and under <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/demo-serializable" data-versioned="true">Serializable isolation</a> when the `optimizer_use_lock_op_for_serializable` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> is `true` ) now locks all <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/column-families" data-versioned="true">column families</a> instead of only the first column family. [#116826](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116826)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-for-update" data-versioned="true">`SELECT FOR UPDATE`</a> under <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/read-committed" data-versioned="true">Read Committed isolation</a> on multi-column-family tables was not locking <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/column-families" data-versioned="true">column families</a> containing only key columns. [#116826](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116826)
- It is now possible to run <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/call" data-versioned="true">`CALL`</a> statements with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/explain" data-versioned="true">`EXPLAIN`</a>. The `EXPLAIN (OPT)` variant will show the body of the procedure, while other variants will only show the procedure name and arguments. [#116274](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116274)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/explain" data-versioned="true">`EXPLAIN`</a> output now contains detailed information about the plans for `CASCADE` actions. [#117719](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117719)

### Operational changes

- Per-node <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-hot-ranges-page" data-versioned="true">hot ranges</a> logging now logs the top 5 hot ranges on the local node instead of the top 5 hot ranges cluster-wide. [#118334](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118334)

### Command-line changes

- Added a new command `cockroach debug enterprise-check-fips`, which diagnoses errors in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/fips" data-versioned="true">FIPS</a> deployments. [#115202](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115202)
- The new flag `--enterprise-require-fips-ready` can be added to any <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-commands" data-versioned="true">`cockroach` command</a> to prevent startup if certain prerequisites for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/fips" data-versioned="true">FIPS</a> compliance are not met. [#115202](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115202)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-workload" data-versioned="true">`cockroach workload`</a> commands now appropriately invoke `.Close` in the case of an error. [#116487](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116487)

### DB Console changes

- Updated the "CPU Time" label on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-runtime-dashboard" data-versioned="true">Runtime Dashboard</a> to "SQL CPU Time" and added clarifications to its tooltip. [#116449](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116449)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page#diagnostics" data-versioned="true">Statement bundles</a> are now enabled for Serverless clusters. [#117529](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117529)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-networking-dashboard" data-versioned="true">Networking Dashboard</a> is enhanced with charts that visualize number of packets received, number of receiving packets with error, number of receiving packets that got dropped, number of packets sent, number of sending packets with error, and number of sending packets that got dropped. [#116712](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116712)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page#explain-plans" data-versioned="true">Explain Plans</a> tab is now shown for the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">Statements</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-insights-page" data-versioned="true">Insights</a> pages, for Serverless clusters. [#118169](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118169)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a durability bug in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#raft" data-versioned="true">Raft log</a> storage, caused by incorrect syncing of filesystem metadata. Previously, it was possible to lose writes of a particular kind ( `AddSSTable` ) that were used by e.g. <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a>. This loss was possible only under power-off or operating system crash conditions. Under such conditions, CockroachDB could enter a crash loop on node restart. In the worst case of a coordinated power-off/crash across multiple nodes this could lead to an unrecoverable loss of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#raft" data-versioned="true">Raft quorum</a>. [#115709](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115709)
- Fixed a bug where large <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">jobs</a> running with execution locality (such as some <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/changefeeds-in-multi-region-deployments#run-a-changefeed-job-by-locality" data-versioned="true">changefeeds</a> ) could result in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/life-of-a-distributed-transaction#gateway" data-versioned="true">gateway</a> node being assigned most of the work, causing performance degradation and cluster instability. [#115388](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115388)
- Fixed a bug that caused node crashes and panics when running <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/insert" data-versioned="true">`INSERT`</a> queries on <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#add-a-unique-index-to-a-regional-by-row-table" data-versioned="true">`REGIONAL BY ROW` tables with `UNIQUE` constraints or indexes</a>. The bug was only present in v23.2.0-beta.1. [#115668](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115668)
- Fixed a bug that existed only in v23.2 alpha and beta versions that could have caused side effects to happen out of order for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/plpgsql" data-versioned="true">PL/pgSQL</a> routines in rare cases. [#115839](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115839)
- Fixed a bug that existed since v23.1 that prevented naming <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type" data-versioned="true">user-defined type (UDT)</a> parameters when dropping a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">user-defined function</a> (or procedure). [#115904](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115904)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-schedules" data-versioned="true">scheduled jobs</a> using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-external-connection" data-versioned="true">external storage providers</a> could fail shortly after node startup. [#115693](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115693)
- Locking tables (e.g., with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-for-update" data-versioned="true">`SELECT FOR UPDATE`</a> ) on the null-extended side of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins" data-versioned="true">outer joins</a> (e.g., the right side of a `LEFT JOIN` ) is now disallowed and returns an error. This improves compatibility with PostgreSQL and prevents ambiguity in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/transaction-layer#concurrency-control" data-versioned="true">locking semantics</a>. This bug has existed since locking with `FOR UPDATE` was introduced. [#115878](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115878)
- Fixed a display bug in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a> where because not all types of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">schema changes</a> are setting the value for the mutation ID, the value of the ID could previously show as "with ID undefined" on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview-dashboard#events-panel" data-versioned="true">Events panel</a>. Now, the notification omits the undefined value (the rest of the event notification is still displayed). [#116518](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116518)
- Fixed the formatting for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/plpgsql" data-versioned="true">PL/pgSQL</a> routines, which could prevent creating a routine with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-procedure#create-a-stored-procedure-that-uses-a-while-loop" data-versioned="true">loop labels</a>, and could prevent some expressions from being <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-logs#redact-logs" data-versioned="true">redacted</a> correctly. The bug only existed in v23.2 alpha and beta releases. [#116713](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116713)
- Fixed a bug that would cause a syntax error during <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-logs#redact-logs" data-versioned="true">redaction</a> of a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/plpgsql" data-versioned="true">PL/pgSQL</a> routine. The bug existed only in v23.2 alpha and beta releases. [#116713](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116713)
- Fixed a bug that would cause syntax errors when attempting to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a> a database with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/plpgsql" data-versioned="true">PL/pgSQL</a> <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/user-defined-functions" data-versioned="true">user-defined functions (UDFs)</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/stored-procedures" data-versioned="true">stored procedures</a>. This bug only affected v23.2 alpha and beta releases. [#116713](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116713)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/update" data-versioned="true">`UPDATE`</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upsert" data-versioned="true">`UPSERT`</a>, and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/insert#on-conflict-clause" data-versioned="true">`INSERT ON CONFLICT`</a> queries are now disallowed under <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/read-committed" data-versioned="true">Read Committed isolation</a> when the table contains a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/check" data-versioned="true">check constraint</a> involving a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/column-families" data-versioned="true">column family</a> that is updated, and the check constraint also involves a column family that is **not** updated, but **is** read. This is a temporary fix to prevent possible violation of the check constraint, and the restriction will be lifted in the future. [#116428](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116428)
- Previously, all `AggHistogram` -powered metrics were not reporting quantiles properly in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a>. This patch fixes the histograms so that the quantiles in DB Console are reported correctly. these histograms were only broken in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview-dashboard" data-versioned="true">DB Console metrics dashboards</a>, but were **not** broken in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/monitoring-and-alerting#prometheus-endpoint" data-versioned="true">Prometheus-compatible endpoint</a>, `/_status/vars`. The list of affected metrics is shown below. [#114506](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114506)
    - `changefeed.message_size_hist`
    - `changefeed.parallel_io_queue_nanos`
    - `changefeed.sink_batch_hist_nanos`
    - `changefeed.flush_hist_nanos`
    - `changefeed.commit_latency`
    - `changefeed.admit_latency`
    - `jobs.row_level_ttl.span_total_duration`
    - `jobs.row_level_ttl.select_duration`
    - `jobs.row_level_ttl.delete_duration`
- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.2 that caused internal errors and panics when certain SQL queries were run with automatic <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page#index-recommendations" data-versioned="true">index recommendation</a> collection enabled. [#117453](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117453)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes" data-versioned="true">Standard indexes</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/inverted-indexes" data-versioned="true">inverted indexes</a> may no longer be created on <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/plpgsql" data-versioned="true">PL/pgSQL</a> `REFCURSOR[]` s columns. `REFCURSOR` columns themselves are not indexable. [#116071](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116071)
- Fixed a bug that prevented database <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a> when the database contained a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/views" data-versioned="true">view</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-procedure" data-versioned="true">routine</a> that referenced a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type" data-versioned="true">user-defined type (UDT)</a> in the body string. For views, this bug was introduced in v20.2, when <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-type" data-versioned="true">user-defined types (UDTs)</a> were introduced. For routines, this bug was introduced in v22.2, when user-defined functions (UDFs) were introduced. [#116841](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116841)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a function resolution error when attempting to use a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">builtin function</a> like `now()` as a formatting argument to a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/plpgsql" data-versioned="true">PL/pgSQL</a> `RAISE` statement. [#116825](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116825)
- Fixed a bug where CDC custom key columns did not function correctly with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-and-configure-changefeeds" data-versioned="true">CDC queries</a>. For example, `CREATE CHANGEFEED WITH key_column=..., unordered AS SELECT * FROM table` now works correctly instead of retrying forever. Note that some functionalities with CDC custom keys are not fully supported, see [#115267](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115267) for more details. [#116967](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116967)
- Fixed a bug in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#raft" data-versioned="true">Raft log</a> truncation that could lead to crash loops, and unrecoverable loss of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#raft" data-versioned="true">quorum</a> in the unlikely worst case that all <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-replica" data-versioned="true">replicas</a> enter this crash loop. The bug manifested when a few things coincided: The cluster was running a bulk write workload (e.g., <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">schema change</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/copy" data-versioned="true">import</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a> ); a log truncation command was running; and the process crashed at an unfortunate moment (e.g., the process was killed, or killed itself for reasons like detecting a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-setup-troubleshooting#disk-stalls" data-versioned="true">disk stall</a> ). [#116574](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116574)
- Fixed the value used for the total runtime on SQL statistics. This was using the wrong value previously, causing the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview#sql-activity" data-versioned="true">SQL Activity</a> page to display values with more than 100%. [#117426](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117426)
- Fixed a bug where trying to set an empty `search_path` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> resulted in an error. [#117557](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117557)
- It is now possible to assign to the parameter of a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/plpgsql" data-versioned="true">PL/pgSQL</a> <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-procedure" data-versioned="true">routine</a>. Previously, attempts to do this would result in a "variable not found" error at routine creation time. In addition, variable shadowing is now explicitly disabled, where previously it would cause an internal error. These bugs existed in the v23.2.0 release and the v23.2 pre-release versions. [#117715](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117715)
- Fixed a bug in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl" data-versioned="true">row-level TTL</a> <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-schedules" data-versioned="true">job</a> that would cause it to skip expired rows if the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/primary-key" data-versioned="true">primary key</a> of the table included columns of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/collate" data-versioned="true">collated string</a> type. This bug was present since the initial release of row-level TTL in v22.2.0. [#117512](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117512)
- Fixed a bug where concurrent <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/grant" data-versioned="true">`GRANT`</a> statements can cause deadlocks. [#117713](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117713)
- CockroachDB can now transparently retry more retryable errors when performing a non-atomic <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/copy" data-versioned="true">`COPY`</a> command. [#117895](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117895)
- Fixed a bug that caused <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/performance-best-practices-overview#dml-best-practices" data-versioned="true">DML statements</a> to fail while a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/hash-sharded-indexes" data-versioned="true">hash-sharded index</a> was being created. The symptom of this bug was an error like `column "crdb_internal_val_shard_16" does not exist`. This bug was present since v23.1.0. [#118215](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118215)
- Previously, CockroachDB could encounter the error `unable to encode table key: *tree.DTSQuery` when operating on columns with the internal `TSQuery` type in some contexts (e.g., when collecting <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics" data-versioned="true">table statistics</a> or when performing a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-clause#eliminate-duplicate-rows" data-versioned="true">`DISTINCT` operation</a> ). This is now fixed. The bug had been present since v23.1 when support for the internal `TSQuery` type was added. [#118321](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118321)
- Previously, in some cases CockroachDB could incorrectly evaluate queries that scanned an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/inverted-indexes" data-versioned="true">inverted index</a> and had a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-clause#where-clause" data-versioned="true">`WHERE` filter</a> in which two sides of the `AND` expression had "similar" expressions (e.g., `ARRAY['str1'] <@ col AND (ARRAY['str1'] && col OR...)` ); this is now fixed. The bug had been present since prior to v22.2. [#118360](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118360)
- Fixed a bug that could cause <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/delete" data-versioned="true">`DELETE`</a> queries sent by the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl" data-versioned="true">row-level TTL</a> <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-schedules" data-versioned="true">job</a> to use a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes" data-versioned="true">secondary index</a> rather than the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/primary-key" data-versioned="true">primary index</a> to find the rows to delete. This could lead to some `DELETE` operations taking a much longer time than they should. This bug was present since v22.2.0. [#118337](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118337)
- Fixed an issue with missing data on SQL statistics, and consequently missing data on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview#sql-activity" data-versioned="true">SQL Activity page</a>, by properly recalculating the value from the current and past hour on the top activity table. [#118378](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118378)
- Internal queries issued by the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/row-level-ttl" data-versioned="true">row-level TTL</a> <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-schedules" data-versioned="true">jobs</a> should now use optimal plans. The bug has been present since at least v22.2. [#118494](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118494)
- Fixed a bug where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> could omit events in rare cases, logging the error `cdc ux violation: detected timestamp... that is less or equal to the local frontier`. This could happen in the following scenario:
    1. A <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-and-configure-changefeeds#enable-rangefeeds" data-versioned="true">rangefeed</a> runs on a follower <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/glossary#cockroachdb-architecture-terms" data-versioned="true">replica</a> that lags significantly behind the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/glossary#cockroachdb-architecture-terms" data-versioned="true">leaseholder</a>.
    2. A transaction commits and removes its <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/transaction-layer#transaction-records" data-versioned="true">transaction record</a> before its <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/transaction-layer#writing" data-versioned="true">intent</a> resolution is applied on the follower.
    3. The follower's <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/transaction-layer#closed-timestamps" data-versioned="true">closed timestamp</a> has advanced past the transaction commit timestamp.
    4. The rangefeed attempts to push the transaction to a new timestamp (at least 10 seconds after the transaction began).
    5. This may cause the rangefeed to prematurely emit a checkpoint before emitting writes at lower timestamps, which in turn may cause the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">changefeed</a> to drop these events entirely, never emitting them. [#118981](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118981)

### Contributors

This release includes 252 merged PRs by 60 authors.

## v23.2.0

Release Date: February 5, 2024

With the release of CockroachDB v23.2, we've added new capabilities to help you migrate, build, and operate more efficiently. See our summary of the most significant user-facing changes under [Feature Highlights](#v23-2-0-feature-highlights).

Experimental downloads are not qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments, whether they are for testing releases or production releases.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v23.2.0
```

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.0 on Github, visit [v23.2.0 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.0).

#### SQL

<table><tbody><tr><th class="center-align" colspan="1" rowspan="2">Feature</th><th class="center-align" colspan="4" rowspan="1">Availability</th></tr><tr><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Ver.</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Self-Hosted</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Dedicated</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Serverless</th></tr><tr><td>Support Read Committed Isolation Level in public preview<br/><br/><a href="/docs/v23.2/read-committed">Read Committed</a> is a weaker transaction isolation level than Serializable and is the default isolation level in databases such as PostgreSQL, Oracle, and SQL Server. Read Committed isolation allows writes to interleave without aborting transactions and prevents writes from blocking reads, thus minimizing query latency and retries caused by read/write contention.</td><td>23.2</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td></tr><tr><td>Improved UDF capabilities<br/><br/><a href="/docs/stable/user-defined-functions">UDFs</a> now support mutations (INSERT, UPDATE, UPSERT, and DELETE).</td><td>23.2</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td></tr><tr><td>Support stored procedures and PL/pgSQL<br/><br/>PL/pgSQL capabilities such as <a href="/docs/v23.2/stored-procedures">stored procedures</a>, conditional logic, loops, and exception handling are now supported, increasing compatibility between CockroachDB and PostgreSQL. An <a href="/docs/stable/licensing-faqs">Enterprise license</a> is required.</td><td>23.2</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td>Delete operation admission control<br/><br/>This feature reduces the potential impact of deleting a large number of rows—directly, as well as implicitly via row-level TTL—on query performance and system stability. For more information, see <a href="/docs/v23.2/admission-control#operations-subject-to-admission-control">Operations subject to admission control</a>.</td><td>23.2</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td></tr><tr><td>Replication admission control<br/><br/>This mechanism automatically paces work for which longer exection times are acceptable (such as index backfills) at the speed of the slowest replica in order to maintain cluster stability and throughput. For more information, see <a href="/docs/v23.2/admission-control#operations-subject-to-admission-control">Operations subject to admission control.</a></td><td>23.2</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td></tr><tr><td>Column Level Encryption<br/><br/>CockroachDB now supports <a href="/docs/v23.2/column-level-encryption">column-level encryption</a> through a set of built-in functions. This feature allows you to encrypt one or more columns in every row of a database table, and can be useful for compliance scenarios such as adhering to PCI or GDPR. An <a href="/docs/stable/licensing-faqs">Enterprise license</a> is required.</td><td>23.2</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td></tr><tr><td>Revoke CREATE privilege by default for public schema<br/><br/>Newer versions of PostgreSQL (15 and above) do not grant the <a href="/docs/v23.2/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges"><code>CREATE</code> privilege</a> by default on the public schema. This change can be disruptive but to preserve Postgres compatibility it is now guarded behind a cluster setting as an opt in feature. This is controlled using a cluster setting: <code>SET CLUSTER SETTING sql.auth.public&#95;schema&#95;create&#95;privilege.enabled=true;</code></td><td>23.2</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td></tr><tr><td>Easily find Default Privileges for a Role<br/><br/>This feature adds a simple syntax to see the <a href="/docs/v23.2/show-default-privileges#show-default-privileges-for-a-grantee">default privileges for a particular grantee</a>. SHOW DEFAULT PRIVILEGES FOR GRANTEE root;</td><td>23.2</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td></tr></tbody></table>

##### Feature detail key

<table><tbody><tr><td>&#42;</td><td>Features marked “All&#42;” were recently made available in the CockroachDB Cloud platform. They are available for all supported versions of CockroachDB, under the deployment methods specified in their row under Availability.</td></tr><tr><td>&#42;&#42;</td><td>Features marked “All&#42;&#42;” were recently made available via migration tools maintained outside of the CockroachDB binary. They are available to use with all supported versions of CockroachDB, under the deployment methods specified in their row under Availability.</td></tr><tr><td><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td>Feature is available for this deployment method of CockroachDB as specified in the icon’s column: CockroachDB Self-Hosted, CockroachDB Dedicated, or CockroachDB Serverless.</td></tr><tr><td><InlineImage alt="Gray circle with horizontal white line (No)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/Eo_circle_grey_white_no-entry.svg" /></td><td>Feature is not available for this deployment method of CockroachDB as specified in the icon’s column: CockroachDB Self-Hosted, CockroachDB Dedicated, or CockroachDB Serverless.</td></tr></tbody></table>

#### Backward-incompatible changes

Before <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upgrade-cockroach-version" data-versioned="true">upgrading to CockroachDB v23.2</a>, be sure to review the following backward-incompatible changes, as well as [key cluster setting changes](#v23-2-0-cluster-settings), and adjust your deployment as necessary.

- The pre-v23.1 output produced by `SHOW RANGES`, `crdb_internal.ranges`, and `crdb_internal.ranges_no_leases` was deprecated in v23.1 and is now replaced by default with output that's compatible with coalesced ranges (anges that pack multiple tables/indexes/partitions into individual ranges). See the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v23.1" data-versioned="true">v23.1 release notes</a> for `SHOW RANGES` for more details. [#102961](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/102961)
- When a deployment is configured to use a time zone for log file output using formats `crdb-v1` or `crdb-v2`, new output log entries cannot be processed by nodes that have not been upgraded to v23.2. [#104265](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104265)
- When customizing the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-sql" data-versioned="true">SQL shell's interactive prompt</a>, the special sequence `%M` now expands to the full host name instead of the combination of host name and port number. To include the port number explicitly, use `%>`. The special sequence `%m` now expands to the host name up to the first period. [#105137](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105137)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-zip" data-versioned="true">`cockroach debug zip`</a> command stores data retrieved from SQL tables in the remote cluster using the TSV format by default. [#107474](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107474)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/protect-changefeed-data" data-versioned="true">`changefeed.protect_timestamp.max_age` cluster setting</a> will only apply to newly created changefeeds in v23.2. For existing changefeeds, you can set the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed#protect-pause" data-versioned="true">`protect_data_from_gc_on_pause`</a> option so that changefeeds do not experience infinite retries and accumulate protected change data. You can use the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-changefeed" data-versioned="true">`ALTER CHANGEFEED`</a> statement to add `protect_data_from_gc_on_pause` to existing changefeeds. [#103539](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103539)
- The direct export of traces to Jaeger and the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `trace.jaeger.agent` have been removed. The direct export functionality had been obsoleted since 2022; it stopped working altogether sometime in 2023 with the following error: `data does not fit within one UDP packet; size 65006, max 65000, spans NN`. Since 2022, Jaeger supports ingestion of traces using OTLP; and CockroachDB has supported emitting traces using OTLP since v22.1. Operators and developers who want to inspect traces are thus invited to use the OTLP protocol instead. The corresponding cluster setting is `trace.opentelemetry.collector`. For a successful deployment, an intermediate OTLP collector/forwarder should be configured. For an example of how to orchestrate the OpenTelemetry collector and Jaeger together using Docker Compose, or how to configure the `otel-collector`, see the more-detailed entry in [v23.2-alpha.3 backward-incompatible changes](#v23-2-0-alpha-3-backward-incompatible-changes). [#111342](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111342)

#### Key Cluster Setting Changes

The following changes should be reviewed prior to upgrading. Default cluster settings will be used unless you have manually set a value for a setting. This can be confirmed by checking the `system.settings` table (`select * from system.settings`) to view the non-default settings.

- The new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `sql.txn.read_committed_syntax.enabled`, controls whether transactions run under `READ COMMITTED` or `SERIALIZABLE` isolation. It defaults to `false`. When set to `true`, the following statements will configure transactions to run under `READ COMMITTED` isolation:
    - `BEGIN TRANSACTION ISOLATION LEVEL READ COMMITTED`
    - `SET TRANSACTION ISOLATION LEVEL READ COMMITTED`
    - `SET default_transaction_isolation = 'read committed'`
    - `SET SESSION CHARACTERISTICS AS TRANSACTION ISOLATION LEVEL READ COMMITTED`

        [#110624](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110624)
- The `sql.txn.read_committed_syntax.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> was renamed to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-sql-txn-read-committed-isolation-enabled" data-versioned="true">`sql.txn.read_committed_isolation.enabled`</a>. [#113833](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113833)
- Users who have the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/grant" data-versioned="true">`CREATEROLE` role option</a> can now grant and revoke role membership in any non-admin role. This change also removes the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">`sql.auth.createrole_allows_grant_role_membership.enabled` cluster setting</a>, which was added in v23.1. In v23.2, the cluster setting is effectively always true. [#104376](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104376)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `sql.metrics.statement_details.gateway_node.enabled` now defaults to false to reduce the number of rows generated in SQL Statistics pages. [#107788](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107788)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `kv.rangefeed.enabled` no longer controls access to `RANGEFEED SQL` commands. Instead, use `feature.changefeed.enabled`. [#110676](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110676)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> related to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/physical-cluster-replication-overview" data-versioned="true">physical cluster replication</a> have been renamed for consistency. For example, `bulkio.stream_ingestion.minimum_flush_interval` is now named `physical_replication.consumer.minimum_flush_interval`. [#111197](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111197)
- CockroachDB now periodically dumps the state of its internal memory accounting system into the `heap_profiler/` directory when a heap profile is taken. To disable this behavior, set the `diagnostics.memory_monitoring_dumps.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> to `false`. [#114998](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114998)
- Introduced the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `kv.gc.sticky_hint.enabled` in v23.1.13. This setting helps expedite <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/storage-layer#garbage-collection" data-versioned="true">garbage collection</a> after range deletions. For example, when a SQL table or index is dropped. `kv.gc.sticky_hint.enabled` is enabled by default and deprecated in v23.2. [#113040](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113040)
- CockroachDB now enables the pacing mechanism in rangefeed closed timestamp notifications, by setting the default `kv.rangefeed.closed_timestamp_smear_interval` cluster setting to 1ms. This makes rangefeed closed timestamp delivery more uniform and less spikey, which reduces its impact on the Go scheduler and, ultimately, foreground SQL latencies. [#103006](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103006)

#### Deprecations

- The `protect_data_from_gc_on_pause` option has been deprecated. This option is no longer needed since changefeed jobs always protect data. [#103539](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103539)
- The `cockroach connect` functionality has been deprecated. [#114241](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114241)

#### Known limitations

For information about new and unresolved limitations in CockroachDB v23.2, with suggested workarounds where applicable, see <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/known-limitations" data-versioned="true">Known Limitations</a>.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is in **Limited Access**.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.2.0-rc.2
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.0-rc.2 on Github, visit [v23.2.0-rc.2 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.0-rc.2).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.0-rc.1...v23.2.0-rc.2](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.0-rc.1...v23.2.0-rc.2)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.2 that caused internal errors and panics when certain queries ran with automatic <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-sql-metrics-statement-details-index-recommendation-collection-enabled" data-versioned="true">index recommendation collection enabled</a>. [#117454](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117454)
- Fixed a bug where mixed-version clusters with both v23.1 and v23.2 nodes could detect a false-positive replica inconsistency in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/global-tables" data-versioned="true">`GLOBAL` tables</a>. [#117341](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117341)

### Contributors

This release includes 12 merged PRs by 9 authors.

href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.2.0-rc.1.windows-6.2-amd64.zip">cockroach-v23.2.0-rc.1.windows-6.2-amd64.zip</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v23.2.0-rc.1.windows-6.2-amd64.zip.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td><td><a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.2.0-rc.1.windows-6.2-amd64.zip">cockroach-sql-v23.2.0-rc.1.windows-6.2-amd64.zip</a><br/>(<a href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.2.0-rc.1.windows-6.2-amd64.zip.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td></tr></tbody></table>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is in **Limited Access**.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.2.0-rc.1
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.0-rc.1 on Github, visit [v23.2.0-rc.1 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.0-rc.1).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.0-beta.3...v23.2.0-rc.1](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.0-beta.3...v23.2.0-rc.1)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Added a SQL function `crdb_internal.fips_ready()` that can be used to verify the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/fips" data-versioned="true">FIPS</a> readiness of the gateway node. [#116281](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116281)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/physical-cluster-replication-overview" data-versioned="true">Physical cluster replication</a> now retries for just over 3 minutes before failing. [#116404](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116404)

### SQL language changes

- `CALL` statements can now be run with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/explain" data-versioned="true">`EXPLAIN`</a>. The `EXPLAIN (OPT)` variant will show the body of the procedure, while other variants will show only the procedure name and arguments. [#116273](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116273)
- Added support for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/import-into" data-versioned="true">`IMPORT INTO`</a> a table that has columns typed as arrays of user-defined types (like <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/enum" data-versioned="true">`ENUM`</a> ). Tables that use multiple user-defined types with the same name but different schemas are still unsupported. [#116360](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116360)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-for-update" data-versioned="true">`SELECT FOR UPDATE`</a> implementation used under Read Committed isolation (and under <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/demo-serializable" data-versioned="true">Serializable isolation</a> when <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">`optimizer_use_lock_op_for_serializable`</a> is set to `true` ) now locks all <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/column-families" data-versioned="true">column families</a> instead of only the first column family. [#116828](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116828)

### Command-line changes

- Added the command <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-commands" data-versioned="true">`cockroach debug enterprise-check-fips`</a> that diagnoses errors in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/fips" data-versioned="true">FIPS</a> deployments. [#116281](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116281)
- Added the flag `--enterprise-require-fips-ready` that can be run with any <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-commands" data-versioned="true">CockroachDB command</a> to prevent startup if certain prerequisites for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/fips" data-versioned="true">FIPS</a> compliance are not met. [#116281](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116281)

### DB Console changes

- Updated the **CPU Time** label to **SQL CPU Time** and added clarification to its tooltip on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview#sql-activity" data-versioned="true">SQL Activity</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-insights-page" data-versioned="true">Insights</a> pages. [#116450](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116450)
- Removed the ID when it is `undefined` from the event description in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview-dashboard#events-panel" data-versioned="true">Metrics Events Panel</a>. [#116519](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116519)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug that caused node crashes and panics when running <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/insert" data-versioned="true">`INSERT`</a> queries on <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/table-localities#regional-by-row-tables" data-versioned="true">`REGIONAL BY ROW`</a> tables with `UNIQUE` constraints or indexes. The bug is only present in version v23.2.0-beta.1. [#116343](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116343)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/update" data-versioned="true">`UPDATE`</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upsert" data-versioned="true">`UPSERT`</a>, and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/insert#on-conflict-clause" data-versioned="true">`INSERT ON CONFLICT`</a> queries are now disallowed under Read Committed isolation when the table contains a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/check" data-versioned="true">`CHECK` constraint</a> involving a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/column-families" data-versioned="true">column family</a> that is updated, and that `CHECK` constraint also involves a column family that is **not** updated, but **is** read. This restriction is a temporary fix to prevent possible violation of the `CHECK` constraint. However, it is important to note that this restriction will be lifted in the future. [#116429](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116429)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-schedules" data-versioned="true">scheduled jobs</a> using <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/use-cloud-storage" data-versioned="true">external storage providers</a> may fail shortly after node startup. [#116205](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116205)
- Fixed the formatting for `plpgsql` routines, which could prevent the creation of a routine with loop labels and could prevent some expressions from being redacted correctly. The bug only existed in alpha and beta versions of v23.2. [#116711](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116711)
- Fixed a bug that would cause a syntax error during redaction of a PL/pgSQL routine. The bug existed only in alpha and beta versions of the v23.2 release. [#116711](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116711)
- Fixed a bug that would cause syntax errors when attempting to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore#restore-a-database" data-versioned="true">restore a database</a> with [PL/pgSQL UDFs](https://www.postgresql.org/docs/current/sql-createfunction) or stored [procedures](https://www.postgresql.org/docs/16/sql-createprocedure). This bug only affected alpha and beta versions of v23.2. [#116711](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116711)
- Fixed a bug in PL/pgSQL where altering the name of a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-sequence" data-versioned="true">sequence</a> or UDT that was used in a [PL/pgSQL function](https://www.postgresql.org/docs/current/sql-createfunction) or [procedure](https://www.postgresql.org/docs/16/sql-createprocedure) could break them. This is only present in v23.2 alpha and beta releases. [#116420](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116420)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-for-update" data-versioned="true">`SELECT FOR UPDATE`</a> under Read Committed isolation on multi-column-family tables was not locking <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/column-families" data-versioned="true">column families</a> containing only key columns. [#116828](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116828)
- Fixed a bug where all `AggHistogram`-powered metrics were not reporting quantiles properly in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">DB Console</a>. The quantiles in the DB Console are now reported correctly. This bug was only present in histograms in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview-dashboard" data-versioned="true">DB Console metrics</a> features, and did **not** affect metrics reporting in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/monitor-cockroachdb-with-prometheus" data-versioned="true">Prometheus-compatible</a> endpoint, `/_status/vars`. The affected metrics were:
    - `changefeed.message_size_hist`
    - `changefeed.parallel_io_queue_nanos`
    - `changefeed.sink_batch_hist_nanos`
    - `changefeed.flush_hist_nanos`
    - `changefeed.commit_latency`
    - `changefeed.admit_latency`
    - `jobs.row_level_ttl.span_total_duration`
    - `jobs.row_level_ttl.select_duration`
    - `jobs.row_level_ttl.delete_duration`

        [#116871](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116871)

### Contributors

This release includes 49 merged PRs by 26 authors.

</Note>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.2.0-beta.3
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.0-beta.3 on Github, visit [v23.2.0-beta.3 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.0-beta.3).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.0-beta.2...v23.2.0-beta.3](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.0-beta.2...v23.2.0-beta.3)

### General changes

- Updated Go version to 1.21.3. [#116098](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116098)

### SQL language changes

- Added the `sql.ttl.default_select_rate_limit` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> and the `ttl_select_rate_limit` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/with-storage-parameter#table-parameters" data-versioned="true">table storage parameter</a> to set the TTL select rate limit. This sets the number of records per table per second per node that can be selected by the TTL job. [#115802](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115802)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug that could result in an incorrect `too few columns` error for queries that use `ANY <array>` syntax with a subquery. [#115592](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115592)
- Fixed a bug that could cause `too few columns` / `too many columns` errors for queries that used `IN` or `NOT IN` with a non-trivial right operand, such as a subquery (rather than a constant tuple). [#115592](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115592)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-index" data-versioned="true">`CREATE INDEX`</a> with expressions could fail on materialized <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/views" data-versioned="true">views</a> when the declarative schema changer was used. [#115522](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115522)
- Fixed a bug that could cause PL/pgSQL routines with `SELECT INTO` syntax to return early. This bug existed only in pre-release versions v23.2.0-beta.1 and v23.2.0-beta.2. [#115676](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115676)
- Fixed a bug that could cause side effects to happen out of order for PL/pgSQL routines in rare cases. This bug existed only in v23.2 alpha versions and previous v23.2 beta versions. [#115840](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115840)
- Previously, in rare cases, CockroachDB could incorrectly evaluate queries with lookup <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins" data-versioned="true">joins</a> where `equality cols are key` when performing lookups on multiple ranges. This could either manifest as a stuck query or result in incorrect output. The bug was introduced in v22.2 and is now fixed. [#115580](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115580)
- Fixed a durability bug in Raft log storage that was caused by incorrect syncing of filesystem metadata. It was possible to lose writes of a particular kind ( `AddSSTable` ) used by (e.g.) `RESTORE`. This loss was possible only under power-off or OS crash conditions. As a result, CockroachDB could enter a crash loop on restart. In the worst case of a coordinated power-off/crash across multiple nodes, this could lead to an unrecoverable loss of quorum. [#115841](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115841)
- Fixed a bug where large jobs running with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/take-locality-restricted-backups" data-versioned="true">`execution locality`</a> option could result in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/sql-layer#gateway-node" data-versioned="true">gateway node</a> being assigned most of the work causing performance degradation and cluster instability. [#115876](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115876)
- Fixed a bug that prevented naming UDT parameters when <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-function" data-versioned="true">dropping a user-defined function</a> (or procedure). This bug has existed since v23.1. [#115905](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115905)
- Locking tables (e.g., with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-for-update" data-versioned="true">SELECT... FOR UPDATE</a> ) on the null-extended side of outer joins (e.g., the right side of a `LEFT JOIN` ) is now disallowed and returns an error. This improves compatibility with PostgreSQL and prevents ambiguity in locking semantics. This bug has existed since locking with `FOR UPDATE` was introduced. [#115879](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115879)

### Contributors

This release includes 26 merged PRs by 20 authors.
