href="https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v23.2.0-beta.2.windows-6.2-amd64.zip.sha256sum">SHA256</a>)</td></tr></tbody></table>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.2.0-beta.2
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.0-beta.2 on Github, visit [v23.2.0-beta.2 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.0-beta.2).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.0-beta.1...v23.2.0-beta.2](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.0-beta.1...v23.2.0-beta.2)

### General changes

- CockroachDB now periodically dumps the state of its internal memory accounting system into the `heap_profiler/` directory when a heap profile is taken. To disable this behavior, set the `diagnostics.memory_monitoring_dumps.enabled` [cluster setting](https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v23.2/cluster-settings) to `false`. [#114998](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114998)
- Multi-level compactions have been disabled to investigate possible performance issues with foreground throughput and latency. [#115481](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115481)

### Enterprise Edition changes

- When using [Physical Cluster Replication](https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v23.2/physical-cluster-replication-overview), you can now [initiate a cutover](https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v23.2/cutover-replication) as of `LATEST` before the initial scan completes. [#115101](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115101)
- Sensitive information such as `api_secret`, `sasl_password`, `client_cert`, and `ca_cert`, is now redacted in output from commands `SHOW CHANGEFEED JOB`, `SHOW CHANGEFEED JOBS`, and [`SHOW JOBS`](https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v23.2/show-jobs). [#115567](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115567)
- The `physical_replication.frontier_lag_nanos` metric and the related DB Console graph have been removed because they sometimes display incorrect information. For [alerting](https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v23.2/physical-cluster-replication-monitoring#prometheus), it is recommended to use the new metric `physical_replication.replicated_time_seconds` metric instead. [#115234](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115234)
- Fixed a bug in [physical cluster replication](https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v23.2/physical-cluster-replication-overview) where replicating from a primary cluster that is on a version prior to v23.2.x to a standby cluster running on v23.2.x could fail because of an undefined builtin function in the primary cluster. [#114257](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114257)

### DB Console changes

- In the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-cdc-dashboard" data-versioned="true">Changeeds dashboard</a>, the **Max Checkpoint Latency** chart title now refers to "Lag" rather than "Latency", to better reflect the intention of the underlying metric, which measures how recently the changefeed was last checkpointed. [#115003](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115003)
- Times on the X-Axis of bar charts in **Statement details** pages are now correctly formatted in UTC. [#115220](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115220)
- In the **SQL Activity** **Transaction Details** page, you can now view a transaction fingerprint ID across multiple applications by specifying the application name in the `appNames` URL `GET` parameter using a comma-separated encoded string of transaction fingerprint IDs. [#115204](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115204)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug that prevented the **Now** button on time range selectors in the DB Console from working as expected when a custom time period was previously selected. [#115514](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115514)
- Fixed a bug that prevented the **SQL Activity** page from showing internal statements when the `sql.stats.response.show_internal.enabled` [cluster setting](https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v23.2/cluster-settings) was set to `true`. [#114824](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114824)
- Fixed a bug where an active replication report update could get stuck in a retry loop on clusters with over 10000 ranges. This could prevent a node from shutting down cleanly. [#114178](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114178)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.1 that could cause an internal error when using the text format (as opposed to binary) when <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sql-grammar#prepare_stmt" data-versioned="true">preparing a statement</a> with a user-defined composite type. [#115064](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115064)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a replica to be stuck processing in a queue's replica set when the replica had recently been removed from purgatory for processing but was destroyed, or the replica's ID changed before being processed. These replicas are now removed from the queue when they are encountered. [#115037](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115037)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sql-grammar#prepare_stmt" data-versioned="true">prepared statement</a> to fail if it references both an `enum` and a table that has undergone a schema change. [#115132](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115132)
- Fixed a bug that could cause cluster version finalization to contend with descriptor lease renewals on large clusters. Descriptor lease renewals previously had a higher priority than cluster upgrade finalization. Finalization now always has a higher priority than descriptor lease renewal. [#115034](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115034)
- Fixed a bug that prevented [backups](https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v23.2/backup) from distributing work evenly across all replicas, including followers, regardless of leaseholder placement. [#115019](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115019)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.2.0-beta.1 that could cause a single composite-typed variable to be incorrectly handled as the target of a PostgreSQL `INTO` clause. [#115404](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115404)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a `BEGIN` statement log to record incorrect information in the `Age` field, which could also cause them to appear erroneously in slow-query logs. [#115259](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115259)

### Performance improvements

- Query planning time has been reduced significantly for some queries in which many tables are joined. [#114445](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114445)

### Contributors

This release includes 91 merged PRs by 35 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.2.0-beta.1
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.0-beta.1 on Github, visit [v23.2.0-beta.1 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.0-beta.1).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.0-alpha.7...v23.2.0-beta.1](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.0-alpha.7...v23.2.0-beta.1)

### SQL language changes

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/copy" data-versioned="true">`COPY`</a> commands now use the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/admission-control#set-quality-of-service-level-for-a-session" data-versioned="true">`background` quality-of-service level</a> by default, which makes `COPY` commands subject to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/admission-control" data-versioned="true">admission control</a>. The new session variable `copy_transaction_quality_of_service` controls the quality-of-service level for `COPY` commands. Previously, `COPY` used the same level as other commands, determined by the `default_transaction_quality_of_service` session variable, which is set to `regular` by default. `regular` is not subject to admission control. [#114535](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114535)

### DB Console changes

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview" data-versioned="true">Overview page</a> now correctly renders the background color for the email signup, which fixes an issue where it was difficult to read the text. [#114547](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114547)
- Fixed a bug where selecting the internal application name prefix `$ internal` from the **Application Name** dropdown on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">**SQL Activity Statements** page</a> was not showing internal queries. The filtering logic will now show if there are statements with the `$ internal` application name prefix. [#114517](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114517)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where an empty <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/overview#architecture-range" data-versioned="true">range</a> corresponding to a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-table" data-versioned="true">`DROP TABLE`</a> did not respect system-level span configurations such as <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/storage-layer#protected-timestamps" data-versioned="true">protected timestamps</a>, which potentially caused reads above the protected timestamp to fail. [#114833](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114833)
- Fixed error handling for `GetFiles` so that it does not cause a nil pointer dereference. [#114830](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114830)

### Contributors

This release includes 33 merged PRs by 21 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.2.0-alpha.7
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.0-alpha.7 on Github, visit [v23.2.0-alpha.7 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.0-alpha.7).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.0-alpha.6...v23.2.0-alpha.7](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.0-alpha.6...v23.2.0-alpha.7)

### SQL language changes

- Previously, if <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/session-variables#use_declarative_schema_changer" data-versioned="true">session variable `use_declarative_schema_changer`</a> was set to `off`, then <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#alter-column" data-versioned="true">`ALTER TABLE... ALTER COLUMN... SET NOT NULL`</a> was run on a column which contained a NULL value, an error with code `23514` ( `check_violation` ) would be returned. Now in this scenario the error returned will have code 23502 ( `not_null_violation` ) to match [PostgreSQL](https://www.postgresql.org/docs/8.4/errcodes-appendix). [#113970](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113970)
- The `sql.txn.read_committed_syntax.enabled` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> was renamed to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings#setting-sql-txn-read-committed-isolation-enabled" data-versioned="true">`sql.txn.read_committed_isolation.enabled`</a>. [#113833](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113833)

### Command-line changes

- The `cockroach connect` functionality has been deprecated. [#114241](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114241)

### DB Console changes

- Previously, the forward arrow button on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page#time-interval" data-versioned="true">time selector</a> would not move the time window forward if the current end time was less than "Now() - time window". For example, with a 10 minute time window, it was not possible to move forward if current end time is less that "Now() - 10 minutes". This caused the forward arrow button to become disabled even though there was more data to display. Now this scenario is handled by the forward arrow button selecting the latest available time window (similar to the **Now** button). [#113907](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113907)

### Bug fixes

- Removed duplication of metrics names on <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview#metrics" data-versioned="true">DB Console Metrics</a> charts' tooltips. [#113728](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113728)
- Fixed a bug that could cause <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-database#add-region" data-versioned="true">ALTER DATABASE... ADD/DROP REGION</a> to hang if <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-start#locality" data-versioned="true">node localities</a> were changed after regions were added. [#114102](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114102)
- A bug in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-logs" data-versioned="true">log configuration</a> code prevented users from setting the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-logs#datetime-field-for-json-format" data-versioned="true">`datetime-format` and `datetime-timezone` log format options</a> (set via the `format-options` structure) within their log configuration. Specifically, when users tried to use these options in `file-defaults` with any <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/log-formats#format-json" data-versioned="true">`json`</a> type log format, the log configuration was previously unable to be parsed due to validation errors. This was because the `file-defaults.format-options` were propagated to the `sinks.stderr.format-options`. `sinks.stderr` only supports a format of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/log-formats#format-crdb-v2-tty" data-versioned="true">`crdb-v2-tty`</a>. Therefore, the incorrectly propagated `format-options`, which are only supported by the `json` log format, were identified as not being supported when validating `sinks.stderr`. This bug is now fixed and the `file-defaults.format-options` are only propagated to `sinks.stderr.format-options` if both of these conditions are true: 1. `file-defaults.format` is one of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/log-formats#format-crdb-v2" data-versioned="true">`crdb-v2`</a> or `crdb-v2-tty`. 2. `sinks.stderr.format-options` are not explicitly set in the log configuration. [#113684](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113684)
- Previously, when executing queries with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/indexes#storing-columns" data-versioned="true">index joins</a> or <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins#lookup-joins" data-versioned="true">lookup joins</a> or both when the ordering needs to be maintained, CockroachDB in some cases would get into a pathological behavior which would lead to increased query latency, possibly by one or two orders of magnitude. This bug was introduced in v22.2 and is now fixed. [#114117](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114117)
- Previously, the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-statistics" data-versioned="true">SHOW STATISTICS command</a> incorrectly required the user to have the admin role. Now, it correctly only requires the user to have any <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#privileges" data-versioned="true">privilege</a> on the table being inspected. [#114449](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114449)
- Fixed a bug that could cause a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">query plan</a> to skip scanning rows from the local region when performing a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins#lookup-joins" data-versioned="true">lookup join</a> with a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/regional-tables#regional-by-row-tables" data-versioned="true">`REGIONAL BY ROW` table</a> as the input. [#114458](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114458)

### Performance improvements

- This change prevents failed requests from being issued on follower nodes that are <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/node-shutdown" data-versioned="true">draining, decommissioning</a> or unhealthy which prevents latency spikes if those nodes later go offline. [#114259](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/114259)

### Contributors

This release includes 95 merged PRs by 33 authors.

Release Date: November 7, 2023

<Warning>

</Warning>

</Note>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.2.0-alpha.6
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.0-alpha.6 on Github, visit [v23.2.0-alpha.6 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.0-alpha.6).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.0-alpha.5...v23.2.0-alpha.6](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.0-alpha.5...v23.2.0-alpha.6)

### General changes

- The CockroachDB Docker image is now based on [Red Hat's ubi9/ubi-minimal image](https://catalog.redhat.com/software/containers/ubi9/ubi-minimal/615bd9b4075b022acc111bf5?architecture=amd64&image=652fc5a903899c8ddcf105be) instead of the ubi8/ubi-minimal image. [#112967](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112967)

### SQL language changes

- Added the built-in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">function</a> `jsonb_array_to_string_array` that converts <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/jsonb" data-versioned="true">`JSONB`</a> array to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/string" data-versioned="true">`STRING`</a> array. [#112865](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112865)
- The built-in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">function</a> `jsonb_array_to_string_array` can now return <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/null-handling" data-versioned="true">`NULL`</a> objects. [#112865](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112865)

### Operational changes

- Introduced the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `kv.gc.sticky_hint.enabled` that helps expediting <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/storage-layer#garbage-collection" data-versioned="true">garbage collection</a> after range deletions. For example, when a SQL table or index is dropped. `kv.gc.sticky_hint.enabled` is enabled by default in v23.2. The setting has been deprecated in v23.2. [#113040](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113040)
- Introduced a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">environment variable</a> that allows an operator to configure the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/storage-layer#compaction" data-versioned="true">compaction</a> concurrency. [#113313](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113313)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-zip" data-versioned="true">Debug zip</a> will now collect the active traces of all running or reverting traceable jobs. This includes <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">restores</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/import" data-versioned="true">imports</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/backup" data-versioned="true">backups</a>, and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/physical-cluster-replication-overview" data-versioned="true">physical cluster replication</a>. [#113172](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113172)

### Cluster virtualization

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges" data-versioned="true">privilege</a> that controls access to `CREATE VIRTUAL CLUSTER` and other virtual cluster management syntax is now called `MANAGEVIRTUALCLUSTER`. [#113076](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113076)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug that could prevent <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a> from working if it was performed during a cluster upgrade. [#112759](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112759)
- Fixed a bug where the opclass for a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/trigram-indexes" data-versioned="true">trigram index</a> is not shown if CockroachDB creates a trigram index and later displays it via <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-create" data-versioned="true">`SHOW CREATE TABLE`</a>. [#113071](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113071)
- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB could incorrectly evaluate <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins#lookup-joins" data-versioned="true">lookup</a> and index <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins" data-versioned="true">joins</a> into tables with at least three <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/column-families" data-versioned="true">column families</a>. This would result in either the `non-nullable column with no value` internal error, or the query would return incorrect results. This bug was introduced in v22.2. [#113105](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113105)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-table#alter-primary-key" data-versioned="true">`ALTER PRIMARY KEY`</a> would incorrectly disable <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/schema-design-indexes" data-versioned="true">secondary indexes</a> while new secondary indexes were being backfilled when using the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">declarative schema changer</a>. [#112627](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112627)
- Fixed a bug where the `unique_constraint_catalog` and `unique_constraint_schema` columns in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/information-schema#referential_constraints" data-versioned="true">`information_schema.referential_constraints`</a> could be incorrect for cross schema or cross database references. [#112739](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112739)
- Fixed a bug in a method that was used by some of the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-jobs" data-versioned="true">jobs</a> observability infrastructure. This method could be triggered if a file was overwritten with a different chunking strategy. [#113290](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113290)
- Fixed a bug where the result of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-create" data-versioned="true">`SHOW CREATE TABLE`</a> for a table that had a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/collate" data-versioned="true">collated string column</a> with a default expression was incorrect because the statement could not be parsed. [#113119](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113119)
- Fixed the SQL activity update job to: avoid conflicts on update, reduce the amount of data cached to only what the overview page requires, and fix the correctness of the top queries. [#112865](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112865)
- Fixed a bug that could prevent <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/physical-cluster-replication-overview" data-versioned="true">physical cluster replication</a> from advancing in the face of some range deletion operations. [#113041](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113041)
- Fixed a bug where <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-type" data-versioned="true">`ALTER TYPE`</a> could get stuck if <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/drop-type" data-versioned="true">`DROP TYPE`</a> was executed concurrently. [#113644](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113644)
- Fixed a bug that could cause internal errors or panics while attempting to forecast <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-statistics" data-versioned="true">statistics</a> on a numeric column. [#113797](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113797)
- Rolled back deletes no longer cause a discrepancy between computed statistics and the actual stored values. [#113766](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113766)

### Performance improvements

- Addressed a performance regression that can happen when the declarative <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/online-schema-changes" data-versioned="true">schema changer</a> is used to create an index with a concurrent workload. [#113725](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113725)

### Contributors

This release includes 117 merged PRs by 49 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.2.0-alpha.5
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.0-alpha.5 on Github, visit [v23.2.0-alpha.5 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.0-alpha.5).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.0-alpha.4...v23.2.0-alpha.5](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.0-alpha.4...v23.2.0-alpha.5)

### SQL language changes

- Added support for the special `OTHERS` condition in PL/pgSQL exception blocks, which allows matching any error code apart from `query_canceled` and `assert_failure`. Note that Class 40 errors ( `40000`, `40001`, `40003`, `40002`, and `40P01` ) cannot be caught either. This is tracked in [#111446](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111446). [#112817](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112817)

### Bug fixes

- Previously, queries with the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/st_union" data-versioned="true">`ST_Union`</a> aggregate function could produce incorrect results in some cases due to the query optimizer performing invalid optimizations. This is now fixed. This bug had been present since the `ST_Union` function was introduced in v20.2.0. [#112780](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112780)

### Contributors

This release includes 27 merged PRs by 17 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.2.0-alpha.4
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.0-alpha.4 on Github, visit [v23.2.0-alpha.4 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.0-alpha.4).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.0-alpha.3...v23.2.0-alpha.4](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.0-alpha.3...v23.2.0-alpha.4)

### General changes

- Updated the `licenses/CCT.txt` file to reflect the latest [Cockroachdb Community License](https://www.cockroachlabs.com/cockroachdb-community-license). [#112494](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112494)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Renamed <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> related to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/physical-cluster-replication-overview" data-versioned="true">physical cluster replication</a> for consistency. For example, `bulkio.stream_ingestion.minimum_flush_interval` is now `physical_replication.consumer.minimum_flush_interval`. [#111197](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111197)

### SQL language changes

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/show-schedules" data-versioned="true">`SHOW SCHEDULES`</a> has two columns that surface the schedule options. These columns have been renamed to align with the documented option names: `on_previous_running` and `on_execution_failure`. [#111759](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111759)
- Added support for the [PLpgSQL `CLOSE` statement](https://www.postgresql.org/docs/current/plpgsql-cursors#PLPGSQL-CURSOR-USING-CLOSE), which allows a PLpgSQL routine to close a cursor with the name specified by a cursor variable. [#111330](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111330)
- When a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a> with `remove_regions` is performed, the restore job will now fail if the object contains a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/table-localities#regional-by-row-tables" data-versioned="true">`REGIONAL BY ROW`</a> table. [#111443](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111443)
- It is now possible to open a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cursors" data-versioned="true">cursor</a> within a PLpgSQL function or procedure with an exception block. If an error occurs, creation of the cursor is rolled back before control reaches the exception handler. [#111735](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111735)
- If a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-schedule-for-backup" data-versioned="true">scheduled backup</a> resumes on a new cluster (e.g., after [physical cluster replication cutover](/docs/v23.2/cutover-replication) or a cluster restore), the backup schedule will pause. The user may <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/resume-schedules" data-versioned="true">resume the schedule</a> without changing it, but should take special care to ensure no other schedule is backing up to the same <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/take-full-and-incremental-backups#backup-collections" data-versioned="true">collection</a>. The user may also want to cancel the paused schedule and start a new one. [#111578](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111578)
- Added support for PLpgSQL [`FETCH`](https://www.postgresql.org/docs/current/plpgsql-cursors#PLPGSQL-CURSOR-USING-FETCH) and [`MOVE`](https://www.postgresql.org/docs/current/plpgsql-cursors#PLPGSQL-CURSOR-USING-MOVE) statements. Similar to SQL `FETCH` / `MOVE` statements, commands that would seek the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cursors" data-versioned="true">cursor</a> backward will fail. In addition, expressions other than constant integers are not yet supported for the `count` option. [#111318](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111318)
- Added support for the [`REFCURSOR`](https://www.postgresql.org/docs/current/plpgsql-cursors#PLPGSQL-CURSOR-DECLARATIONS) data type. `REFCURSOR` is a special string type that is used to handle cursors. PLpgSQL cursor declarations are required to use a variable of type `REFCURSOR`, and the name of a cursor can be passed to and from a PLpgSQL function or procedure. [#111392](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111392)
- Added two changes to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-for-update" data-versioned="true">`FOR UPDATE`</a>:
    - Multiple `FOR UPDATE` clauses on fully parenthesized queries are now disallowed. For example, the following statements are now disallowed:

        ```sql
        (SELECT 1 FOR UPDATE) FOR UPDATE;
        SELECT * FROM ((SELECT 1 FOR UPDATE) FOR UPDATE) AS x;
        ```

        Whereas statements like the following are still allowed:

        ```sql
        SELECT * FROM (SELECT 1 FOR UPDATE) AS x FOR UPDATE;
        SELECT (SELECT 1 FOR UPDATE) FOR UPDATE;
        ```

        This does not match PostgreSQL, which allows all of these, but does match CockroachDB behavior for `ORDER BY` and `LIMIT`.
    - `FOR UPDATE` is now allowed on statements with `VALUES` in the `FROM` list, or as a subquery. For example, the following statements are now allowed:

        ```sql
        SELECT (VALUES (1)) FOR UPDATE;
        SELECT * FROM (VALUES (1)) AS x FOR UPDATE;
        ```

        Using `FOR UPDATE` directly on `VALUES` is still disallowed:

        ```sql
        VALUES (1) FOR UPDATE; (VALUES (1)) FOR UPDATE;
        INSERT INTO t VALUES (1) FOR UPDATE;
        ```

        This matches PostgreSQL. [#111258](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111258)
- `FOR UPDATE` is now permitted on some queries that were previously disallowed. Queries that use the following operations are now allowed to have `FOR UPDATE OF` as long as the prohibited operation is in a subquery not locked by the `FOR UPDATE OF`:
    - `UNION`
    - `INTERSECT`
    - `EXCEPT`
    - `DISTINCT`
    - `GROUP BY`
    - `HAVING`
    - Aggregations
    - <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/window-functions" data-versioned="true">Window functions</a>

        For example, the following query is now allowed because the subquery using the prohibited operations is not affected by the `FOR UPDATE OF`:

        ```sql
        SELECT * FROM t, (SELECT DISTINCT 0, 0 UNION SELECT a, count(*) FROM t GROUP BY a HAVING a > 0) AS u FOR UPDATE OF t;
        ```

        This matches PostgreSQL. [#111258](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111258)
- Identifiers after numeric constants that are not separated by whitespace are now disallowed to match PostgreSQL 15 behavior. [#112021](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112021)
- Added the new column `contention_type` to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/crdb-internal" data-versioned="true">`crdb_internal.transaction_contention_events`</a> table. This column indicates the type of <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/performance-best-practices-overview#transaction-contention" data-versioned="true">transaction contention</a> encountered. Current values are `LOCK_WAIT` and `SERIALIZATION_CONFLICT`. [#111685](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111685)
- Changed the error message: `statement error cannot execute FOR UPDATE in a read-only transaction` to `statement error cannot execute SELECT FOR UPDATE in a read-only transaction` to match PostgreSQL. [#112138](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112138)
- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> `optimizer_use_lock_op_for_serializable`, which when set enables a new implementation of `SELECT FOR UPDATE`. This new implementation of `SELECT FOR UPDATE` acquires row locks **after** any joins and filtering, and always acquires row locks on the primary index of the table being locked. This more closely matches <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/select-for-update" data-versioned="true">`SELECT FOR UPDATE`</a> behavior in PostgreSQL, but at the cost of more round trips from gateway node to replica leaseholder. Under read-committed isolation (and other isolation levels weaker than serializable), CockroachDB will always use this new implementation of `SELECT FOR UPDATE` regardless of the value of `optimizer_use_lock_op_for_serializable` to ensure correctness. [#112138](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112138)

### Operational changes

- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `server.http.base_path` that controls the redirection of the browser after successful login with <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/sso-db-console" data-versioned="true">OIDC SSO</a>. It is unlikely that this setting would need adjustment. However, it is helpful in cases where CockroachDB is running behind a load balancer or proxy that serves CockroachDB under a subpath, such as `https:// <hostname>/crdb/`. In those cases, it is necessary for the browser to redirect to `/ crdb` after login instead of `/`, which has always been the hard-coded default. [#111283](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111283)

### Cluster virtualization

- The following settings can now only be set from the system virtual cluster:
    - All the `physical_replication.*` settings
    - `server.rangelog.ttl`
    - `timeseries.storage.*`

        [#111769](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111769)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> `cluster.organization` and `enterprise.license` can now only be set via the system virtual cluster. Attempting to set them from any other virtual cluster results in an error. [#111788](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111788)
- A new flag `--internal-rpc-port-range` allows operators to specify the port range used by virtual clusters for node-to-node communication. Users implementing <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/physical-cluster-replication-overview" data-versioned="true">physical cluster replication</a> or cluster virtualization public preview features should use this flag if they require the `cockroach` processes to only communicate using ports in a known port range. [#111798](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111798)
- Two guardrails are available to system operators to help with users upgrading from a deployment without cluster virtualization enabled to a deployment using cluster virtualization. This is intended to help in cases where the user is not connected to the correct SQL interface to perform certain configuration operations. There are two guardrails included:
    - The `sql.restrict_system_interface.enabled` cluster setting encourages users to use a virtual cluster for their application workload. When set, certain common operations that end users may execute to set up an application workload are disallowed, such as running DDL statements or modifying an application level cluster setting. Users will receive an error similar to:

        ```text
        ERROR: blocked DDL from the system interface SQLSTATE: 42501 HINT: Object creation blocked via sql.restrict_system_interface.enabled to prevent likely user errors. Try running the DDL from a virtual cluster instead.
        ```
    - The `sql.error_tip_system_interface.enabled` cluster setting enhances errors reported when a user mistakenly uses a storage-level SQL feature within any virtual cluster besides the system virtual cluster. For example, when attempting to modify a cluster setting that was previously at the application level, an error like the following occurs:

        ```text
        NOTICE: ignoring attempt to modify "kv.rangefeed.enabled"
        HINT: The setting is only modifiable by the operator.
        Normally, an error would be reported, but the operation is silently accepted here as configured by "sql.error_tip_system_interface.enabled".
        ```
    - For a cluster setting that was always system-level, an error like the following occurs:

        ```text
        ERROR: cannot modify storage-level setting from virtual cluster
        SQLSTATE: 42501
        HINT: Connect to the system interface and modify the cluster setting from there.
        ```

        [#111568](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111568)
- The predefined config profiles related to cluster virtualization now automatically set the new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> `sql.restrict_system_interface.enabled` and `sql.error_tip_system_interface.enabled`. [#111568](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111568)
- The hidden `--secondary-tenant-port-offset` option has been removed. Users who were previously using this option should use `--internal-rpc-port-range` instead. [#112050](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112050)
- Added support for automatic finalization of a virtual cluster's version upgrade. A new setting `cluster.auto_upgrade.enabled` was added to enable and disable automatic cluster version upgrade (finalization). It will be used in automatic upgrade of both the storage cluster and its virtual clusters. [#102427](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/102427)

### Command-line changes

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-zip" data-versioned="true">`cockroach debug zip`</a> has an additional flag that is default off `include-running-job-traces` that will enable collecting the in-flight traces of traceable jobs, such as <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/backup" data-versioned="true">backup</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">restore</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/import-into" data-versioned="true">import</a>, <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/physical-cluster-replication-overview" data-versioned="true">physical cluster replication</a> and dump them in a `jobs/` subdirectory in the zip. [#112644](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112644)

### DB Console changes

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-jobs-page" data-versioned="true">**Jobs** table</a> will now correctly display timestamps for creation, last modified, and the completed time fields. [#110366](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110366)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-insights-page" data-versioned="true">transaction insight details</a> will show the following details when CockroachDB has information on a transaction execution with a `40001` error code and it has captured the conflicting transaction meta details (only available if the transaction had not yet committed at the time of execution). A section called `Failed Execution` will appear when this information is available and it will contain:
    - Blocking transaction execution ID
    - Blocking transaction fingerprint ID
    - Conflict location
    - Database, table, and index names [#111873](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111873)
- Added progressive loading functionality to the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-databases-page" data-versioned="true">Databases page</a>. [#110901](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110901)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/physical-cluster-replication-overview" data-versioned="true">physical cluster replication</a> where the primary cluster would not be able to take <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/take-full-and-incremental-backups" data-versioned="true">backups</a> when a primary cluster node was unavailable. [#111337](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111337)
- Fixed a bug in <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-insights-page" data-versioned="true">transaction insight details</a> where it was possible to see the contention details of other transactions. Now, CockroachDB will only surface contention details for the current transaction. [#111867](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111867)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-replication-zones" data-versioned="true">Voter constraints</a> will now be satisfied by promoting existing non-voters. Previously, there was a bug where voter constraints were never satisfied due to all existing replicas being considered necessary to satisfy a replica constraint. [#111609](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111609)
- Fixed a bug where `indoption` inside `pg_index` was not properly encoded causing clients to be unable to decode it as `int2vector`. [#111911](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111911)
- This patch fixes an issue where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> fails to honor the `statement_timeout` session setting when generating constrained index scans for queries with large `IN` lists or `= ANY` predicates on multiple index key columns, which may lead to an out of memory condition on the node. [#111979](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111979)
- This patch fixes a performance issue in join queries with a `LIMIT` clause, where the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> may fail to push a `WHERE` clause filter into a join due to how the `LIMIT` operation is internally rewritten. This causes a full scan of the table referenced in the filter. [#110593](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110593)
- Fixed a bug that caused internal errors during query optimization in rare cases. The bug has been present since version v2.1.11, but it is more likely to occur in version v21.2.0 and later, though it is still rare. The bug only presents when a query contains `min` and `max` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators#aggregate-functions" data-versioned="true">aggregate functions</a>. [#112255](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/112255)

### Performance improvements

- This patch adds support for insert fast-path uniqueness checks on <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/table-localities#regional-by-row-tables" data-versioned="true">`REGIONAL BY ROW`</a> tables where the source is a `VALUES` clause with a single row. This results in a reduction in latency for single-row inserts to `REGIONAL BY ROW` tables and hash-sharded `REGIONAL BY ROW` tables with unique indexes. [#111822](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111822)

This release includes 213 merged PRs by 51 authors. We would like to thank the following contributors from the CockroachDB community:

- Finn Mattis (first-time contributor)
- craig

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.2.0-alpha.3
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.0-alpha.3 on Github, visit [v23.2.0-alpha.3 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.0-alpha.3).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.0-alpha.2...v23.2.0-alpha.3](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.0-alpha.2...v23.2.0-alpha.3)

### Backward-incompatible changes

- The direct export of traces to Jaeger and the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `trace.jaeger.agent` have been removed. The direct export functionality had been obsoleted since 2022; it stopped working altogether sometime in 2023 with the following error: `data does not fit within one UDP packet; size 65006, max 65000, spans NN`. Since 2022, Jaeger supports ingestion of traces using OTLP; and CockroachDB has supported emitting traces using OTLP since v22.1. Operators and developers who want to inspect traces are thus invited to use the OTLP protocol instead. The corresponding cluster setting is `trace.opentelemetry.collector`. For a successful deployment, an intermediate OTLP collector/forwarder should be configured.
    - You can orchestrate the OpenTeletry collector and Jaeger together using Docker Compose by adapting the following example:

        ```yaml
        otel-collector:
          image: otel/opentelemetry-collector-contrib
          container_name: otel-collector
          volumes:
            - ./otel-collector-config.yaml:/etc/otelcol-contrib/config.yaml
          ports:
            - 1888:1888 # pprof extension
            - 8888:8888 # Prometheus metrics exposed by the collector
            - 8889:8889 # Prometheus exporter metrics
            - 13133:13133 # health_check extension
            - 4317:4317 # OTLP gRPC receiver
            - 4318:4318 # OTLP http receiver
            - 55679:55679 # zpages extension

        jaeger:
          image: jaegertracing/all-in-one
          container_name: jaeger
          ports:
            - "16685:16685"
            - "16686:16686"
            - "14250:14250"
            - "14268:14268"
            - "14269:14269"
            - "6831:6831/udp"
          environment:
            - COLLECTOR_ZIPKIN_HTTP_PORT=9411
            - COLLECTOR_OTLP_ENABLED=true
        ```
    - To configure the `otel-collector`, you can adapt this example:

        ```yaml
        receivers:
          otlp: # the OTLP receiver the app is sending traces to
            protocols:
              grpc:
              http:

        processors:
          batch:

        exporters:
          otlp/jaeger: # Jaeger supports OTLP directly
            endpoint: http://jaeger:4317
            tls:
              insecure: true

        service:
          pipelines:
            traces/dev:
              receivers: [otlp]
              processors: [batch]
              exporters: [otlp/jaeger]
        ```

To use this configuration, unset Jaeger via `SET CLUSTER SETTING trace.jaeger.agent=''`, and then set the OTLP collector using `SET CLUSTER SETTING trace.opentelemetry.collector='localhost:4317'`.

### Enterprise edition changes

- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-and-configure-changefeeds" data-versioned="true">Changefeeds</a> now support the `confluent-cloud://` sink scheme. This scheme can be used to connect to Kafka hosted on Confluent Cloud. The scheme functions identically to Kafka, but it has it's own authentication parameters. Namely, it requires `api_key` and `api_secret` to be passed as parameters in the sink URI. They must be URL encoded. An example URI is: `'confluent-cloud://pkc-lzvrd.us-west4.gcp.confluent.cloud:9092?api_key=<KEY>&api_secret=<SECRET>'`. By default, the options `tls_enabled=true`, `sasl_handshake=true`, `sasl_enabled=true`, and `sasl_mechanism=PLAIN` are applied. For more information about authenticating with Confluent Cloud, see https://docs.confluent.io/platform/current/security/security_tutorial.html#overview. The sink scheme still supports non-authentication parameters such as `topic_name` and `topic_prefix`. It also supports the standard Kafka changefeed options (ex. `kafka_sink_config` ). [#111368](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111368)

### SQL language changes

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/restore" data-versioned="true">`RESTORE`</a> option `strip_localities`, which was added in [#110606](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110606), has been renamed to `remove_regions`. This option will lead to a "region-less restore"; it is used to strip the locality and region information from a backup when there are mismatched cluster regions between the backup's cluster and the target cluster. Note that a restore using this option will fail if the backup's cluster had <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/multiregion-overview#table-locality" data-versioned="true">`REGIONAL BY ROW`</a> table localities. This is because the `RESTORE` statement has a contract that all tables must be available to serve writes once it finishes. [#111356](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111356)
- Added initial support for executing the PLpgSQL `OPEN` statement, which allows a PLpgSQL routine to create a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cursors" data-versioned="true">cursor</a>. Currently, opening bound or unnamed cursors is not supported. In addition, `OPEN` statements cannot be used in a routine with an exception block. [#110709](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110709)
- Added support for declaring bound <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cursors" data-versioned="true">cursors</a>, which associate a query with a cursor in a PLpgSQL routine before it is opened. [#111092](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111092)
- The `SELECT FOR SHARE` and `SELECT FOR KEY SHARE` statements previously did not acquire any locks. Users issuing these statements would expect them to acquire shared locks (multiple readers allowed, but no writers). This patch switches over the behavior to acquire such read locks when the user has selected the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/transactions#isolation-levels" data-versioned="true">`READ COMMITTED` isolation level</a>. For serializable transactions, we default to the previous behavior, unless the `enable_shared_locking_for_serializable` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session setting</a> is set to `true`. [#109638](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109638)
- When a PLpgSQL exception handler catches an error, it now rolls back any changes to database state that occurred within the block. Exception blocks are not currently permitted to catch <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/common-errors#restart-transaction" data-versioned="true">`40001`</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/common-errors#result-is-ambiguous" data-versioned="true">`40003`</a> errors. [#110998](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110998)
- Added support for unnamed PLpgSQL <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cursors" data-versioned="true">cursors</a>, which generate a unique name when no cursor name was specified. [#111329](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111329)
- Fixed a bug that caused CockroachDB to stop collecting new statistics about <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page#statement-fingerprint-page" data-versioned="true">Statement fingerprints</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-transactions-page" data-versioned="true">Transaction fingerprints</a>. [#111613](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111613)
- Make the `max_event_frequency` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metric</a> visible for public documentation and usage. This is the maximum event frequency at which we sample executions for telemetry. [#111594](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111594)

### Operational changes

- Added the following <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metrics</a> for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer#raft" data-versioned="true">Raft</a> proposals and reproposals: `raft.commands.proposed`, `raft.commands.reproposed.unchanged`, and `raft.commands.reproposed.new-lai`. [#111272](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111272)
- Removed the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `spanconfig.store.enabled` and the ability to use the `COCKROACH_DISABLE_SPAN_CONFIGS` environment variable. [#110253](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110253)
- Renamed the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metric</a> `fluent.sink.conn.errors` to `log.fluent.sink.conn.errors`. The addition of the `log.` prefix was to better group together logging-related metrics. The behavior and purpose of the metric remains unchanged. [#111126](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111126)
- Set the Metric Type metadata on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metric</a> `log.fluent.sink.conn.errors`. Previously, the Metric Type was incorrectly left unset. Note that this is an update to the metric's metadata; the behavior and purpose of the metric remains unchanged. [#111126](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111126)
- Added a new <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metric</a> `log.buffered.messages.dropped`. Buffered network logging sinks have a `max-buffer-size` attribute, which determines, in bytes, how many log messages can be buffered. Any `fluent-server` or `http-server` log sink that makes use of a `buffering` attribute in its configuration (enabled by default) qualifies as a buffered network logging sink. If this buffer becomes full, and an additional log message is sent to the buffered log sink, the buffer would exceed this `max-buffer-size`. Therefore, the buffered log sink drops older messages in the buffer to handle, in order to make room for the new. `log.buffered.messages.dropped` counts the number of messages dropped from the buffer. Note that the count is shared across all buffered logging sinks. [#111126](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111126)
- Added the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/metrics" data-versioned="true">metric</a> `log.messages.count`. This metric measures the count of messages logged on the node since startup. Note that this does not measure the fan-out of single log messages to the various configured <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/configure-logs#set-logging-levels" data-versioned="true">logging sinks</a>. This metric can be helpful in understanding log rates and volumes. [#111126](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111126)
- Added the `file-based-headers` field found in the `http-defaults` section of the log config, which accepts 'key-filepath' pairs. This allows values found at filepaths to be updated without restarting the cluster by sending `SIGHUP` to notify that values need to be refreshed. [#111235](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111235)
- Added the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `kv.snapshot.ingest_as_write_threshold`, which controls the size threshold below which snapshots are converted to regular writes. It defaults to `100KiB`. [#110943](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110943)

### Cluster virtualization

- The name of the virtual cluster that the SQL client is connected to can now be inspected via the SQL <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/set-vars" data-versioned="true">session variable</a> `virtual_cluster_name`. [#111565](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111565)

### Command-line changes

- The following <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster settings</a> have been renamed; the previous names remain available for backward-compatibility. [#109415](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109415)

    <table><thead><tr><th>Previous name</th><th>New Name</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>server.shutdown.drain&#95;wait</code></td><td><code>server.shutdown.initial&#95;wait</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>server.shutdown.lease&#95;transfer&#95;wait</code></td><td><code>server.shutdown.lease&#95;transfer&#95;iteration.timeout</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>server.shutdown.query&#95;wait</code></td><td><code>server.shutdown.transactions.timeout</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>server.shutdown.connection&#95;wait</code></td><td><code>server.shutdown.connections.timeout</code></td></tr><tr><td><code>server.shutdown.jobs&#95;wait</code></td><td><code>server.shutdown.jobs.timeout</code></td></tr></tbody></table>

### DB Console changes

- Fixed an error on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview#sql-activity" data-versioned="true">SQL Activity page</a> when there was a workload, and then the workload stopped so that no queries ran against the database in the last hour. [#111420](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111420)
- On the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview#metrics" data-versioned="true">Metrics page</a>, now the information about which metric is used to create each chart is available on the chart's tooltip. [#111469](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111469)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed the error message that is returned when the user attempts to drop an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/enum" data-versioned="true">`ENUM`</a> value that is used at least twice in an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/array" data-versioned="true">`ARRAY`</a> column. [#111354](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111354)
- Added a check for values before using `mean` on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">Plan Details page</a>, fixing a crash. [#111472](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111472)
- Fixed the metric name for `Schema Registry Registrations` on the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overview#metrics" data-versioned="true">Metrics page</a>. [#111469](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111469)
- Fixed a panic that could occur if a query used a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/string" data-versioned="true">string</a> larger than 2^31-1 bytes. This was triggered by attempting to <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/import" data-versioned="true">import</a> a 2.7 GiB CSV file. [#111627](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111627)
- Fixed a bug where `atttypmod` in `pg_attribute` was not populated for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/timestamp" data-versioned="true">`TIMESTAMP`</a> / <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/interval" data-versioned="true">`INTERVAL`</a> types, which meant that ORMs could not know the precision of these types properly. [#111400](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111400)

### Contributors

This release includes 130 merged PRs by 43 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.2.0-alpha.2
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.0-alpha.2 on Github, visit [v23.2.0-alpha.2 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.0-alpha.2).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v23.2.0-alpha.1...v23.2.0-alpha.2](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.0-alpha.1...v23.2.0-alpha.2)

### Security updates

- The `SIGHUP` signal now clears the cached expiration times for <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-cert#how-security-certificates-work" data-versioned="true">client certificates</a> that are reported by the `security.certificate.expiration.client` metric. [#110726](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110726)

### General changes

- Increased the maximum permitted value of the `COCKROACH_RPC_INITIAL_WINDOW_SIZE` environment variable to 64MB. In conjunction with tuning your operating system's maximum TCP window size, this can increase the throughput that Raft replication can sustain over high latency network links. [#111255](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111255)

### SQL language changes

- The `discard` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/logging-overview" data-versioned="true">log message</a> is now limited to once per minute by default. The message now includes both the number of transactions and the number of statements that were discarded. [#110805](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110805)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">cluster setting</a> `kv.rangefeed.enabled` no longer controls access to `RANGEFEED SQL` commands. Instead, use `feature.changefeed.enabled`. [#110676](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110676)
- SQL commands that were previously limited to the `admin` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges" data-versioned="true">system privilege</a> can now be used by users with the `VIEWCLUSTERMETADATA` or `REPAIRCLUSTERMETADATA` system privilege, depending on whether the operation is read-only or modifies state. [#110084](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110084)
- Added a `last_error` column to the `cluster_execution_insights`, `node_execution_insights`, `cluster_txn_execution_insights`, and `node_txn_execution_insights` tables. These columns contain error messages for failed executions. [#110565](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110565)
- The new backup option `updates_cluster_monitoring_metrics` tracks the timestamp of the last backup failure due to a KMS error. This option is disabled by default. [#104634](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104634)
- The new restore option `strip_localities` optionally strips the locality information from a backup when restoring to a cluster with different regions than the source cluster.

Restoring a cluster or database that contains regional-by-row tables, or restoring a regional-by-row table, requires you to modify the database:

- To restore a cluster with regional-by-row tables, you must drop the zone config of the database, then drop the type `d.public.crdb_internal_region`.
- To restore a database that contains regional-by-row tables, or to restore a regional-by-row table, you must drop the type `d.public.crdb_internal_region`.
- You must alter the `crdb_region` column to set the default region for newly-written rows.
- You must discard the previous zone config, which contains outdated information, such as that related to the partitions and constraints after the restore. This column specifies each row's home region and is a prefix to the table's primary key. Stripping localities does not modify this column, because it would require the entire table to be written.

This change is part of a larger effort, and this feature is subject to change.

[#110606](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110606)

- Added a check to disallow queries that use predicate locking, since explicit uniqueness checks are not yet supported under Read Committed isolation. `INSERT`, `UPDATE`, and `UPSERT` statements against some `REGIONAL BY ROW` tables will fail under Read Committed isolation with the following error:

```shell
  unimplemented: explicit unique checks are not yet supported under read committed isolation SQLSTATE: 0A000
```

For more details about which `REGIONAL BY ROW` tables are affected, refer to [Issue #110873](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/issues/110873).

[#110879](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110879) - The `created` field produced by `SHOW STATISTICS` has been updated from `TIMESTAMP` to `TIMESTAMPTZ`. Statistic creation times are now displayed in the session time zone if it is set. [#110753](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110753)

### Operational changes

- Removed the node-level `engine.stalls` timeseries metric. This metric has not been updated for several releases. [#110936](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110936)

### DB Console changes

- The legend is now always displayed on charts in DB Console Metrics pages. In addition, when you select an item from the legend that represents a single line in the chart, that line is selected in the chart. [#110809](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110809)
- When collecting a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-statement-diag" data-versioned="true">statement bundle</a>, you can now filter by a specific <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page#explain-plans" data-versioned="true">plan gist</a> or collect diagnostics for all plan gists. [#110931](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110931)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-statements-page" data-versioned="true">Statement</a> and <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-transactions-page" data-versioned="true">Transaction</a> detail pages now include an **Error Message** row. Users with the `VIEWACTIVITY` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges" data-versioned="true">system privilege</a> can view the full error message, and users with the `VIEWACTIVTYREDACTED` system privilege can view the redacted error message. If a user has both privileges, `VIEWACTIVITYTREDACTED` &#96; takes precedence. [#110849](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110849)
- A new dashboard in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-sql-dashboard" data-versioned="true">SQL Dashboard page</a> tracks how often distributed queries with errors were rerun using the "rerun as local" mechanism, as well as how often those reruns failed. the number of times distributed queries that resulted in errors were rerun as local as well as when those reruns failed. The "rerun as local" mechanism is new in v23.2 and is enabled by default. For more information, contact your Cockroach Labs account representative. [#110619](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110619)
- The DB Console [Insights page](https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v23.2/ui-insights-page) now shows the error message when a transaction fails at the `COMMIT` stage. [#110898](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110898)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/ui-overload-dashboard" data-versioned="true">Overload Dashboard page</a> now includes the following graphs to monitor <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/admission-control" data-versioned="true">admission control</a>:
    - **IO Overload** - Charts normalized metric based on admission control target thresholds. Replaces **LSM L0 Health** graph which used raw metrics.
    - **KV Admission Slots Exhausted** - Replaces **KV Admission Slots** graph.
    - **Flow Tokens Wait Time: 75th percentile** - Use to monitor the new replication admission control feature.
    - **Requests Waiting For Flow Tokens** - Use to monitor the new replication admission control feature.
    - **Blocked Replication Streams** - Use to monitor the new replication admission control feature. [#110135](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110135)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a race condition in the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/replication-layer" data-versioned="true">Replica lifecycle</a> that could result in a failed SQL request when the request could have been successfully retried. [#110806](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110806)
- Fixed a bug where a <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-table" data-versioned="true">`CREATE TABLE`</a> command with an `IDENTITY` column did not properly propagate the type of the column into the sequence. [#110621](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110621)
- Fixed a panic when decoding a gist in a foreign database that does not contain a table referred to by the gist. [#110966](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110966)
- A synthetic `dropped` column have been added to the `pg_attribute` table. This column tracks the attribution numbers for dropped attributions, to work around issues with ORMs that are not designed to handle gaps in attribution numbering in the `pg_attribute` table. [#111019](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111019)
- Fixed a rare internal error in the `unnest` and `information_schema._pg_expandarray` <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/functions-and-operators" data-versioned="true">built-in functions</a> where passed string arguments could be cast to an array. [#110956](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110956)
- External connection URLs now accept the scheme `azure-blob` for connections to Azure Blob Storage and the scheme `azure-kms` for connections to Azure KMS. For backward compatibility, schemes `azure` and `azure-storage` schemes continue to work for connections to Azure Blob Storage. [#111217](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111217)
- Fixed a bug where vectorized `COPY FROM` could produce a plan with more than one RenderNodes, when only zero or one should be allowed. This could result in multiple render nodes in a table with a hash sharded primary key. [#111284](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111284)
- Fixed a bug in DB Console's Statement Diagnostic page that could cause the page to crash if the response was larger than 50 KB. The page now keeps pulling results until no maximum size errors are encountered. [#111128](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111128)
- Fixed a bug where DB Console instances proxied at different subpaths that use OIDC pointed to an incorrect relative OIDC login path. [#111240](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111240)
- Fixed a bug where changing the setting `server.telemetry.hot_ranges_stats.interval` had no effect. [#111305](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111305)

### Performance improvements

- Fixed a performance bug that could result in rewriting a 128-MB file each time a store file is created, renamed, or removed when <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/security-reference/encryption#encryption-at-rest" data-versioned="true">Encryption At Rest</a> is enabled on a large store with many small files. [#111069](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111069)
- Improved compaction heuristics to mitigate read amplification growth and admission control throttling when processing large deletes, such as during node decommissioning, replica rebalancing, or when dropping tables. [#111277](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/111277)

### Contributors

This release includes [157 merged PRs by 54 authors](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v23.2.0-alpha.1...2111b61b2d7c789bc03b1e9392062df80c779075).

## v23.2.0-alpha.1

Release Date: September 26, 2023

### Downloads

<Warning>
CockroachDB v23.2.0-alpha.1 is a testing release. Testing releases are intended for testing and experimentation only, and are not qualified for production environments and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
</Warning>

<Note>
Experimental downloads are not qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments, whether they are for testing releases or production releases.
</Note>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image:

- The ARM image is **Experimental** and not yet qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
- The Intel image is **Generally Available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v23.2.0-alpha.1
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v23.2.0-alpha.1 on Github, visit [v23.2.0-alpha.1 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v23.2.0-alpha.1).

### Backward-incompatible changes

- The pre-v23.1 output produced by `SHOW RANGES`, `crdb_internal.ranges`, and `crdb_internal.ranges_no_leases` was deprecated in 23.1 and is now replaced by default with output that's compatible with coalesced ranges (i.e., ranges that pack multiple tables/indexes/partitions into individual ranges). See the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/releases/v23.1" data-versioned="true">v23.1 release notes</a> for `SHOW RANGES` for more details. [#102961](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/102961)
- When a deployment is configured to use a time zone (new feature) for log file output using formats `crdb-v1` or `crdb-v2`, it becomes impossible to process the new output log files using the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-merge-logs" data-versioned="true">`cockroach debug merge-logs` command</a> from a previous version. The newest `cockroach debug merge-logs` code must be used instead. [#104265](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104265)
- When customizing the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-sql" data-versioned="true">SQL shell's interactive prompt</a>, the special sequence `%M` now expands to the full host name instead of the combination of host name and port number. To include the port number explicitly, use `%>`. The special sequence `%m` now expands to the host name up to the first period. [#105137](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105137)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cockroach-debug-zip" data-versioned="true">`cockroach debug zip`</a> command stores data retrieved from SQL tables in the remote cluster using the TSV format by default. [#107474](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107474)
- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/protect-changefeed-data" data-versioned="true">`changefeed.protect_timestamp.max_age` cluster setting</a> will only apply to newly created changefeeds in v23.2. For existing changefeeds, you can set the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/create-changefeed#protect-pause" data-versioned="true">`protect_data_from_gc_on_pause`</a> option so that changefeeds do not experience infinite retries and accumulate protected change data. You can use the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/alter-changefeed" data-versioned="true">`ALTER CHANGEFEED`</a> statement to add `protect_data_from_gc_on_pause` to existing changefeeds. [#103539](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103539)
- The `changefeed.new_pubsub_sink_enabled` cluster setting is now enabled by default, which improves changefeed throughput. With this setting enabled, the top-level fields in JSON-encoded messages are capitalized: `{Key:..., Value:..., Topic:...}`. After upgrading to CockroachDB v23.2, you may need to reconfigure downstream systems to parse the new message format. If you disable this setting, changefeeds emitting to Pub/Sub sinks with JSON-encoded events have the top-level message fields all lowercase: `{key:..., value:..., topic:...}`.

### Security updates

- Users who have the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/grant" data-versioned="true">`CREATEROLE` role option</a> can now grant and revoke role membership in any non-admin role. This change also removes the <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cluster-settings" data-versioned="true">`sql.auth.createrole_allows_grant_role_membership.enabled` cluster setting</a>, which was added in v23.1. In v23.2, the cluster setting is effectively always true. [#104376](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104376)

### General changes

- You can now set <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/start-a-local-cluster-in-docker" data-versioned="true">Docker</a> command arguments using the `COCKROACH_ARGS` environment variable. [#98899](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98899)
- Extended the [`/api/v2/nodes` API endpoint](/docs/api/cluster/v2) with a `storeMetrics` field. [#98208](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/98208)
- CockroachDB would previously use separate <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/architecture/distribution-layer" data-versioned="true">ranges</a> for each table, index, or partition. This is no longer true. It is possible now to have multiple tables, indexes, and partitions get packed into the same range.
