- Fixed a bug where an `ALTER TABLE... ADD CONSTRAINT CHECK...` statement that utilized a user-defined function in the `CHECK` could cause a validation error. [#110130](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110130)
- Fixed a bug where `RESET (ttl_expire_after)` could incorrectly remove `ttl_expiration_expression`. [#110252](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110252)
- Fixed a bug where the `format_type` built-in did not honor `typemod` information for array types, leading to incorrect output. [#110900](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110900)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v22.2 that incorrectly allowed users without the `EXECUTE` privilege to execute a user-defined function. [#107587](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107587)

### Performance improvements

- The <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/cost-based-optimizer" data-versioned="true">optimizer</a> now plans inverted index scans for queries using `IN` or the `=` operators without the fetch val ( `->` ) operator. For example: `json_col = '{"b":"c"}' OR json_col IN ('"a"', '1')` [#101178](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/101178)
- Queries that have subqueries in equality expressions are now more efficiently planned by the optimizer. [#100881](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/100881)
- Query planning time has been reduced for some queries with multiple <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/joins" data-versioned="true">joins</a>. [#102011](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/102011)
- CockroachDB now enables the pacing mechanism in rangefeed closed timestamp notifications, by setting the default `kv.rangefeed.closed_timestamp_smear_interval` cluster setting to 1ms. This makes rangefeed closed timestamp delivery more uniform and less spikey, which reduces its impact on the Go scheduler and, ultimately, foreground SQL latencies. [#103006](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103006)
- Some large, long-running <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/insert" data-versioned="true">`INSERT`</a> statements now perform less work during their commit phase and can run faster. [#103241](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103241)
- Ranges now only quiesce after 3 seconds without proposals, to avoid frequent unquiescence which incurs an additional Raft proposal. This is configurable via the `COCKROACH_QUIESCE_AFTER_TICKS` environment variable, which defaults to 6. [#103266](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103266)
- SQL statements that must clean up intents from many different previously abandoned transactions now do so moderately more efficiently. [#103265](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/103265)
- The optimizer can now avoid a grouping stage in more cases when de-duplicating the input to an <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/upsert" data-versioned="true">`UPSERT`</a> or `INSERT... ON CONFLICT` statement. [#105206](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105206)
- The optimizer can now eliminate joins in more cases. [#105214](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/105214)
- CockroachDB now improves the time to disk space reclamation when deleting rows. Previously, in scenarios where rows had large variations in row size, it was possible for disk space to not be reclaimed after MVCC garbage collection deleted the rows. [#104539](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/104539)
- CockroachDB now has improved disk space reclamation heuristics, making disk space reclamation more timely. [#106177](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106177)
- `bool_and` and `bool_or` aggregates will now scale linearly instead of quadratically when used as a window function with a non-shrinking window, [#106477](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106477)
- CockroachDB now has reduced lock contention on `ssmemstorage.RecordStatement`. This is useful for workloads that execute the same statement concurrently on the same SQL instance. [#106860](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/106860)
- The optimizer now produces more efficient query plans in some cases for queries with subqueries and user-defined functions. [#107133](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107133)
- The default Raft entry cache size has been increased from 16 MB to 1/256 of system memory with a minimum of 32 MB, divided evenly between all stores. This can be configured using the `COCKROACH_RAFT_ENTRY_CACHE_SIZE` environment variable. [#107424](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107424)
- CockroachDB now automatically collects table statistics on the `system.jobs` table, which will enable the optimizer to produce better query plans for internal queries that access the `system.jobs` table. This may result in better performance of the system. [#108139](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/108139)
- The impact of high concurrency blind writes to the same key on goroutine scheduling latency was reduced. [#109349](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109349)
- <a href="/docs/VERSION_PLACEHOLDER/change-data-capture-overview" data-versioned="true">Changefeeds</a> to Webhook or Pub/Sub endpoints now support much higher throughput [#109351](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109351)
- This release improved the cost of resolving a user-defined enum type that has many values. [#109394](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109394)
- Queries that compare collated strings now use less memory and may execute faster. [#110066](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110066)
- Added a scheduler based rangefeed processor which improves rangefeed and changefeed performance for very large tables. The new processor is disabled by default, but can be enabled by setting `kv.rangefeed.scheduler.enabled` cluster setting to `true`. [#107553](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/107553)
- This release disables `sql.defaults.zigzag_join.enabled` by default. [#110214](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/110214)

### Build changes

- Go has been upgraded to 1.20.8. [#109773](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/109773)
- The top-level `Makefile` was replaced by a stub `GNUmakefile` which defers its behavior to `dev`. The common targets `make [all]`, `make test`, and `make install` remain for compatibility with most UNIX installation guides. The previous `make` rules remain available via `make -C build/GNUmakefile.obsolete`. [#84565](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/84565)

### Contributors

This release includes 3208 merged PRs by 124 authors.
